## **Fighter**  
*Mercenary | Enforcer | Paranormal Combatant | Gladiator*  

> *"Violence is the last refuge of the incompetent. Fortunately, I'm very competent."*  
> — **Lena Duval, The Iron Pact**  

### **Thematic Overview**  
Fighters are the backbone of Concord City’s conflicts. Whether serving as corporate enforcers, mercenary bruisers, or paranormal hunters, they rely on honed combat skills rather than magic. Some train in Thaumatech combat schools, while others survive through sheer grit and experience.
- Fighters excel in armed and unarmed combat, adapting to the demands of the battlefield.  
- Their training may come from corporate security forces, criminal syndicates, or old-school martial traditions.  
- Paranormal entities, street gangs, and corporations alike employ skilled fighters as elite enforcers.  
- A fighter’s style reflects their origins, from brutal street brawling to disciplined tactical combat.  

### **Creating a Fighter**  
- Did you train under a formal institution like a Thaumatech security firm or House d’Este’s royal guard?  
- Were you a street brawler, a syndicate enforcer, or a war veteran seeking employment in Concord City?  
- What drives you to keep fighting—survival, justice, revenge, or ambition?  


## **Class Features**  
As a **Fighter**, you gain the following class features.

### **Hit Points**  
- **Hit Dice:** *1d10 per Fighter level*  
- **Hit Points at 1st Level:** *10 + Constitution modifier*  
- **Hit Points at Higher Levels:** *1d10 (or 6) + Constitution modifier per level after 1st*  

### **Proficiencies**  
- **Armor:** *All armor, shields*  
- **Weapons:** *Simple weapons, martial weapons*  
- **Tools:** *None*  
- **Saving Throws:** *Strength, Constitution*  
- **Skills:** *Choose two from Acrobatics, Athletics, History, Insight, Intimidation, Perception, and Survival*  

### **Equipment**  
You start with the following equipment, in addition to any granted by your background:  
- *(a)* a chainblade or *(b)* a battle rifle and 20 rounds  
- *(a)* a sidearm and 10 rounds or *(b)* two daggers  
- *(a)* a reinforced vest or *(b)* a combat jacket  
- An explorer’s pack  


## **Class Table**  
| Level | Proficiency Bonus | Features |  
|:-:|:-:|:--|  
| 1st | +2 | Fighting Style, Second Wind |  
| 2nd | +2 | Action Surge (one use) |  
| 3rd | +2 | Martial Archetype |  
| 4th | +2 | Ability Score Improvement |  
| 5th | +3 | Extra Attack |  
| 6th | +3 | Ability Score Improvement |  
| 7th | +3 | Martial Archetype Feature |  
| 8th | +3 | Ability Score Improvement |  
| 9th | +4 | Indomitable (one use) |  
| 10th | +4 | Martial Archetype Feature |  
| 11th | +4 | Extra Attack (2) |  
| 12th | +4 | Ability Score Improvement |  
| 13th | +5 | Indomitable (two uses) |  
| 14th | +5 | Ability Score Improvement |  
| 15th | +5 | Martial Archetype Feature |  
| 16th | +5 | Ability Score Improvement |  
| 17th | +6 | Action Surge (two uses), Indomitable (three uses) |  
| 18th | +6 | Martial Archetype Feature |  
| 19th | +6 | Ability Score Improvement |  
| 20th | +6 | Extra Attack (3) |  

\page

## **Class Abilities**  
### **Fighting Style (Level 1)**  
You adopt a particular style of fighting as your specialty. Choose one of the following options:
- **Dueling:** +2 bonus to damage with one-handed weapons.
- **Great Weapon Fighting:** Reroll 1s and 2s on damage dice for two-handed melee weapons.
- **Defense:** +1 AC while wearing armor.
- **Archery:** +2 bonus to attack rolls with ranged weapons.

### **Second Wind (Level 1)**  
You can use a bonus action to regain hit points equal to *1d10 + your Fighter level*. Once you use this feature, you must finish a short or long rest before you can use it again.  

### **Action Surge (Level 2)**  
On your turn, you can take one additional action. Once used, you must finish a short or long rest before using it again. At 17th level, you can use it twice per rest.  

---

## **Subclasses: Martial Archetypes**  
At **3rd level**, you choose a subclass that defines your approach to combat. Choose from the following options: 


# Fighter Archetypes  

---

### **Street Enforcer (Corporate Muscle & Gang Enforcer)**
*"You have two choices: pay up, or let me break something."*  

#### **Features & Playstyle**  
- **Excels in intimidation, brutal takedowns, and tactical beatdowns.**  
- Focuses on **close-quarters combat, crowd control, and interrogation.**  
- Common among **corporate security, debt collectors, and underground enforcers.**  

#### **Archetype Abilities**  
| Level | Feature |  
|-------|---------|  
| 3rd | **Tactical Intimidation** – Gain proficiency in Intimidation. When you hit a creature with a melee attack, you can force them to make a Wisdom saving throw or become frightened for 1 round. |  
| 7th | **Riot Control** – If you successfully shove or grapple a creature, you can make an additional melee attack as a bonus action. |  
| 10th | **Unshakable Authority** – Gain resistance to charm and fear effects. Your Intimidation checks automatically succeed against creatures below your Fighter level. |  
| 15th | **Brutal Compliance** – When a creature you have grappled attempts to break free, you can use your reaction to make an attack against them. |  
| 18th | **Final Warning** – Once per long rest, when you reduce a creature to 0 HP, you can instead leave them at 1 HP and force them to surrender. |  

---

### **Urban Warlord (Master of Tactical Combat & City Warfare)**
*"The battlefield isn’t a field anymore. It’s the streets."*  

#### **Features & Playstyle**  
- **Masters of urban combat, gang warfare, and tactical engagements.**  
- Excels at **using cover, terrain, and urban spaces to outmaneuver enemies.**  
- Common among **mercenary leaders, underground generals, and veteran survivors.**  

#### **Archetype Abilities**  
| Level | Feature |  
|-------|---------|  
| 3rd | **Tactical Positioning** – When you move at least 10 feet, you gain +2 AC until the start of your next turn. |  
| 7th | **Commanding Presence** – You can use a bonus action to give an ally within 30 feet an additional reaction until the start of your next turn. |  
| 10th | **Urban Guerrilla** – When attacking from cover, you deal an additional 1d6 damage. If an enemy attacks you while you have cover, you can use your reaction to move 10 feet without provoking opportunity attacks. |  
| 15th | **Master of the City** – You gain expertise in Survival and Stealth while in urban environments. Your movement is never hindered by debris, crowds, or barricades. |  
| 18th | **Tactical Strike** – Once per long rest, you can take two turns in the first round of combat. |  

---

### **Iron Curtain (Heavy Security & Armored Warfare)**
*"Nothing gets past me. Nothing."*  

#### **Features & Playstyle**  
- **Turns defense into an unstoppable force.**  
- Focuses on **armor reinforcement, damage mitigation, and battlefield control.**  
- Common among **corporate bodyguards, riot officers, and armored mercenaries.**  

\page

#### **Archetype Abilities**  
| Level | Feature |  
|-------|---------|  
| 3rd | **Unmovable** – While wearing heavy armor, gain advantage on Strength saving throws and cannot be forcibly moved against your will. |  
| 7th | **Fortified Stance** – If you do not move on your turn, you gain +2 AC and resistance to all damage until the start of your next turn. |  
| 10th | **Reactive Guard** – When an ally within 5 feet is attacked, you can use your reaction to impose disadvantage on the attack roll. |  
| 15th | **Unbreakable Shell** – While wearing heavy armor, reduce all non-magical damage taken by 3. |  
| 18th | **Impenetrable Bastion** – Once per long rest, you can become immune to all damage except force for one turn. |  

---

### **Bullet Dancer (Gunfighter & Precision Marksman)**
*"One shot, one kill. That’s all I need."*  

#### **Features & Playstyle**  
- **Specializes in firearms, rapid targeting, and precision kills.**  
- Excels at **long-range marksmanship, mobility, and critical hits.**  
- Common among **corporate assassins, snipers, and rogue bounty hunters.**  

#### **Archetype Abilities**  
| Level | Feature |  
|-------|---------|  
| 3rd | **Gunslinger’s Reflexes** – You can reload firearms as a bonus action and gain a +1 bonus to attack rolls with ranged weapons. |  
| 7th | **Deadeye Focus** – When you aim at a target for a full round (no movement), your next shot automatically lands as a critical hit if it hits. |  
| 10th | **Mobile Sniper** – Your movement speed increases by 10 feet. You ignore movement penalties from difficult terrain. |  
| 15th | **Trick Shot** – Once per short rest, you can fire a special shot that blinds, stuns, or disarms a target. |  
| 18th | **Lethal Precision** – Once per long rest, if you hit a creature with a ranged weapon, you can force them to make a Constitution saving throw or instantly drop to 0 HP. |  

---

### **Pit Fighter (Brutal Unarmed Combat & Arena Dominance)**
*"They locked me in the cage. They should’ve locked themselves out."*  

#### **Features & Playstyle**  
- **Masters of unarmed combat, grappling, and raw physical dominance.**  
- Gains **brutal melee techniques, enhanced durability, and relentless aggression.**  
- Common among **illegal fight club champions, underground gladiators, and enhanced street brawlers.**  

#### **Archetype Abilities**  
| Level | Feature |  
|-------|---------|  
| 3rd | **Brutal Strikes** – Your unarmed strikes deal 1d8 damage and count as magical. |  
| 7th | **Bonebreaker** – When you score a critical hit, the target must succeed on a Constitution saving throw or suffer a lingering injury (GM’s discretion). |  
| 10th | **Unstoppable Will** – You gain resistance to bludgeoning damage and cannot be knocked prone while standing. |  
| 15th | **Arena Veteran** – When reduced to 0 HP, you can make a Constitution saving throw (DC 15). On success, you remain at 1 HP instead. |  
| 18th | **The Last One Standing** – Once per long rest, if you are the only conscious fighter in combat, you regain all your hit points and gain advantage on all attacks for 1 minute. |  

---

### **Anomaly Hunter (Monster Killer & Paranormal Specialist)**
*"I know what lurks in the dark. I know how to kill it."*  

#### **Features & Playstyle**  
- **Masters of fighting supernatural creatures and anomalies.**  
- Uses **specialized combat techniques to neutralize paranormal threats.**  
- Common among **A.S.T.R.A.L. operatives, rogue hunters, and private-sector exorcists.**  

#### **Archetype Abilities**  
| Level | Feature |  
|-------|---------|  
| 3rd | **Supernatural Tactician** – Gain proficiency in Arcana and advantage on Insight checks against non-humanoids. |  
| 7th | **Hunter’s Strike** – When attacking an entity classified as “otherworldly” (GM’s discretion), your first attack each turn deals an additional 1d8 force damage. |  
| 10th | **Ward Against the Unseen** – You gain resistance to necrotic and psychic damage. |  
| 15th | **Anti-Anomaly Strike** – Your weapon attacks ignore resistance and immunity to non-magical damage. |  
| 18th | **Final Containment** – Once per long rest, you can force an anomaly into a weakened state, preventing it from using special abilities for 1 minute. |  

\page

### **The Executor (Corporate Hitman & Professional Assassin)**  
*"No witnesses. No mistakes. No mercy."*  

#### **Features & Playstyle**  
- **Masters of assassination, precision kills, and cold efficiency.**  
- Focuses on **stealth, critical hits, and lethal single-strike takedowns.**  
- Common among **corporate black ops, government-sanctioned killers, and elite bounty hunters.**  

#### **Archetype Abilities**  
| Level | Feature |  
|-------|---------|  
| 3rd | **Executioner’s Strike** – If you hit a surprised or unaware enemy, you automatically score a critical hit. |  
| 7th | **Perfected Stealth** – Gain proficiency in Stealth. You can move at full speed while sneaking without penalty. |  
| 10th | **No Loose Ends** – Once per long rest, when you drop an enemy to 0 HP, you can erase all evidence of their existence, preventing resurrection or tracking. |  
| 15th | **Lethal Efficiency** – When you land a critical hit, you roll an additional damage die. |  
| 18th | **Instant Silence** – Once per long rest, you can use your reaction to **vanish completely for 1 minute,** leaving no trace of your presence. |  

---

### **The Juggernaut (Unstoppable Industrial Tank & Walking Fortress)**  
*"Hit me again. See what happens."*  

#### **Features & Playstyle**  
- **Masters of damage absorption, sheer endurance, and unstoppable force.**  
- Becomes harder to kill the more damage they take.  
- Common among **riot officers, ex-military juggernauts, and corporate wrecking machines.**  

#### **Archetype Abilities**  
| Level | Feature |  
|-------|---------|  
| 3rd | **Unstoppable Charge** – If you move at least 10 feet before making an attack, your hit deals extra damage equal to your Strength modifier. |  
| 7th | **Damage Threshold** – You reduce all damage taken by 3 while wearing heavy armor. |  
| 10th | **Shock Absorption** – When hit by a melee attack, you can use your reaction to gain temporary HP equal to half the damage taken. |  
| 15th | **Indomitable Stance** – If you are reduced to 0 HP, you remain conscious until the end of your next turn. You can use this once per long rest. |  
| 18th | **Immortal Machine** – Once per long rest, you can ignore exhaustion and all negative conditions for 10 minutes, making you immune to fear, charm, stun, and paralysis. |  

---

### **The Arcane Gunslinger (Experimental Firearm Tactician & Magitech Sharpshooter)**  
*"Bullets run out. But my tricks never do."*  

#### **Features & Playstyle**  
- **Combines magic with firearms, using enchanted bullets and spell-powered rounds.**  
- Excels at **ranged combat, mobility, and arcane-infused gunplay.**  
- Common among **rogue corporate weapons testers, outlaw spellshooters, and experimental marksmen.**  

#### **Archetype Abilities**  
| Level | Feature |  
|-------|---------|  
| 3rd | **Spellshot** – You can infuse firearms with magic, allowing you to fire ranged spell attacks. |  
| 7th | **Runed Ammunition** – You gain the ability to craft special bullets that deal force, lightning, or fire damage. |  
| 10th | **Ricochet Trickshot** – Once per short rest, you can curve a bullet around cover to hit an unseen target. |  
| 15th | **Arcane Overload** – Once per long rest, you can fire a charged shot that **forces an enemy to make a Constitution save or take double damage.** |  
| 18th | **Bulletstorm** – You can make three ranged attacks instead of two when you use the Attack action. |  

---

### **The Riot Breaker (Corporate Security & Suppression Specialist)**  
*"When diplomacy fails, I don’t."*  

#### **Features & Playstyle**  
- **Masters of crowd control, non-lethal combat, and area suppression.**  
- Excels at **disabling, incapacitating, and breaking organized resistance.**  
- Common among **riot police, corporate peacekeepers, and security enforcers.**  

#### **Archetype Abilities**  
| Level | Feature |  
|-------|---------|  
| 3rd | **Shock Baton Mastery** – You gain proficiency in non-lethal weapons. Your melee attacks can impose the **Stunned** condition on a failed Constitution save. |  
| 7th | **Tactical Crowd Control** – When hitting an enemy, you can push them back 10 feet without using a shove action. |  
| 10th | **Gas Dispersal** – Once per short rest, you can deploy an **area of tear gas** that causes blindness and coughing fits. |  
| 15th | **Suppressing Strikes** – When you hit a creature, it has disadvantage on attack rolls against targets other than you. |  
| 18th | **Unyielding Authority** – Creatures of CR 10 or lower automatically fail their saving throw against your control abilities. |  

\page

### **The Revenant Striker (Haunted Fighter & Deathless Duelist)**  
*"I fell. I rose again. And now I hunt."*  

#### **Features & Playstyle**  
- **Refuses to die, gaining supernatural resilience and vengeful strength.**  
- Uses **haunted abilities, ghost-like combat, and unrelenting pursuit.**  
- Common among **revenant assassins, resurrected warriors, and those who refuse the grave.**  

#### **Archetype Abilities**  
| Level | Feature |  
|-------|---------|  
| 3rd | **Death’s Favor** – If you fall below half HP, you gain advantage on all attack rolls until the end of combat. |  
| 7th | **Ethereal Step** – Once per short rest, you can phase out of existence for one round, becoming immune to damage. |  
| 10th | **Vengeful Strikes** – When hit by an attack, your next melee strike deals double damage. |  
| 15th | **Ghostbound Fury** – While below 10 HP, all attacks against you have disadvantage, and your attacks have advantage. |  
| 18th | **Final Stand** – Once per long rest, when reduced to 0 HP, you stay active for 1 minute before finally collapsing. |  

---

### **The Blackguard (Doomed Warrior & Last Bastion of Power)**  
*"They say I can’t win. I say they haven’t met me yet."*  

#### **Features & Playstyle**  
- **Survivors of impossible odds, wielding sheer determination as a weapon.**  
- Excels in **turning desperate situations into victories.**  
- Common among **war veterans, broken heroes, and those who refuse fate.**  

#### **Archetype Abilities**  
| Level | Feature |  
|-------|---------|  
| 3rd | **Defiant Stance** – When surrounded by at least two enemies, you gain a +2 bonus to AC. |  
| 7th | **Unyielding Will** – If reduced to 0 HP, you can roll a Constitution save (DC 15) to stay at 1 HP instead. |  
| 10th | **Fury of the Doomed** – If you are the last conscious ally, you gain resistance to all damage. |  
| 15th | **Final Gambit** – Once per long rest, you can sacrifice half your remaining HP to double all damage dealt for one round. |  
| 18th | **Legend Never Dies** – If you fall in battle, an ally within 30 feet gains temporary HP equal to half your maximum HP. |  

---

## **Multiclassing**  
If your campaign allows multiclassing, use the following rules for a **Fighter** multiclass character.  

### **Ability Score Minimums**  
- Strength 13 or Dexterity 13  

### **Proficiencies Gained**  
- Light armor, medium armor, shields, simple weapons, martial weapons  

---

## **Quick Build**  
You can make a **Fighter** quickly by following these suggestions:  
- Choose **Human or Orc** for the best thematic fit.  
- Pick the **Soldier** or **Mercenary Veteran** background.  
- Prioritize **Strength or Dexterity**, followed by **Constitution**.  
- Take a melee weapon and a defensive armor set for optimal early game survival.

## **Monk**  
*Martial Adept | Paranormal Ascetic | Reality Harmonizer | Cybernetic Mystic*  

> *"True control is not over others, but over yourself."*  
> — **Master Tian, Order of the Fractured Path**  

### **Thematic Overview**  
Monks in Concord City are more than warriors—they are **masters of body and mind**, using discipline to transcend the limits of reality itself. Some refine their abilities through **corporate-funded enhancement programs**, while others follow **ancient traditions reinterpreted for a modern world**. Some claim to have developed their abilities through **paranormal enlightenment**, while others use cybernetic implants to replicate supernatural feats.
- Monks are **warriors of discipline, blending combat mastery with supernatural insight**.  
- Some serve as **paranormal detectives, corporate bodyguards, or spiritual guides**.  
- Others live in the shadows, seeking **absolute control over their mind and body**.  
- Their ki is **a fusion of disciplined energy, psychic control, or even latent anomalies**.  

### **Creating a Monk**  
- Were you trained in a hidden monastery, a corporate dojo, or through sheer personal will?  
- Do you believe in spiritual enlightenment, or is your power purely practical?  
- How do you view Concord City—something to be protected, or something to be transcended?  


## **Class Features**  
As a **Monk**, you gain the following class features.

### **Hit Points**  
- **Hit Dice:** *1d8 per Monk level*  
- **Hit Points at 1st Level:** *8 + Constitution modifier*  
- **Hit Points at Higher Levels:** *1d8 (or 5) + Constitution modifier per level after 1st*  

### **Proficiencies**  
- **Armor:** *None*  
- **Weapons:** *Simple weapons, short swords*  
- **Tools:** *Choose one artisan’s tool or one gaming set*  
- **Saving Throws:** *Strength, Dexterity*  
- **Skills:** *Choose two from Acrobatics, Athletics, History, Insight, Religion, and Stealth*  

### **Equipment**  
You start with the following equipment, in addition to any granted by your background:  
- *(a)* a pair of reinforced gloves or *(b)* a monofilament staff  
- *(a)* an armored bodysuit or *(b)* a martial artist’s gi  
- *(a)* a street guide or *(b)* a cybernetic data-link  
- A set of meditation beads or a focus implant  

\page

## **Class Abilities**  
### **Martial Arts (Level 1)**  
You can use Dexterity instead of Strength for unarmed strikes and monk weapons. Your unarmed strikes deal damage based on your **Martial Arts die**.

### **Ki (Level 2)**  
You harness **paranormal energy, cybernetic impulses, or pure willpower** as ki points. You can spend these points to:  
- **Flurry of Blows:** Make two unarmed strikes as a bonus action.  
- **Step of the Wind:** Dash or Disengage as a bonus action.  
- **Patient Defense:** Take the Dodge action as a bonus action.  

### **Deflect Missiles (Level 3)**  
When hit by a ranged weapon attack, you can reduce its damage. If reduced to 0, you can spend **1 ki point** to throw it back.


## **Subclasses: Monastic Traditions**  
At **3rd level**, you choose a Monastic Tradition that defines your approach to martial arts.

---

### **Way of Concrete**  
*"The city is my monastery. The streets are my training ground."*  

#### **Features & Playstyle**  
- **Masters of raw urban power, using walls, structures, and sheer resilience as weapons.**  
- Fights with **reinforced fists, brutal efficiency, and an unbreakable body.**  
- Common among **underground monks, forgotten disciples, and the Concrete Monastery.**  

#### **Monastic Abilities**  
| Level | Feature |  
|-------|---------|  
| 3rd | **Brutalist Strikes** – Your unarmed attacks deal additional damage when striking against walls, floors, or solid surfaces. If you force an enemy into a structure, they take extra damage equal to your Wisdom modifier. |  
| 6th | **Unbreakable Form** – Gain resistance to bludgeoning damage. If an effect would knock you prone, you can make a Strength saving throw to remain standing. |  
| 11th | **The City's Grip** – While in urban environments, you can run across vertical surfaces indefinitely and climb sheer walls without a check. |  
| 17th | **Concrete Sentinel** – Once per long rest, you can temporarily **merge with a building or structure**, gaining complete cover and becoming undetectable for 1 minute. |  

---

### **Way of the Kaisoku Blade**  
*"Strike first. Strike last. Strike with purpose."*  

#### **Features & Playstyle**  
- **Specializes in katana combat, using speed and deadly precision.**  
- Excels at **single-strike execution, battlefield control, and overwhelming speed.**  
- Common among **Kaisoku Enclave warriors, master duelists, and corporate assassins.**  

\page

#### **Monastic Abilities**  
| Level | Feature |  
|-------|---------|  
| 3rd | **Kaisoku Draw** – When rolling initiative, you may make a katana attack as a free action before combat begins. If you kill an enemy with this strike, you gain an additional action. |  
| 6th | **Blade Reflexes** – When an enemy within 5 feet misses an attack, you can use your reaction to strike them with your katana. |  
| 11th | **Wind Slash** – You can make an attack that cuts through the air, striking all enemies in a 15-foot line. |  
| 17th | **One Cut, One Kill** – Once per long rest, if you hit a creature with a melee weapon attack, you can force them to make a Constitution saving throw. On a failure, they are reduced to 0 HP instantly. |  

---

### **Way of the Static Fist**  
*"Speed is everything. Hesitation is death."*  

#### **Features & Playstyle**  
- **Uses electrical currents and extreme reflexes to enhance combat.**  
- Excels at **high-speed movement, rapid counterattacks, and shocking strikes.**  
- Common among **cybernetic warriors, corporate enforcers, and energy channelers.**  

#### **Monastic Abilities**  
| Level | Feature |  
|-------|---------|  
| 3rd | **Charged Blows** – Your unarmed strikes deal additional lightning damage equal to your Wisdom modifier. |  
| 6th | **Surge Step** – When moving at least 10 feet, you can deal extra thunder damage on your next melee attack. |  
| 11th | **Instant Reflexes** – You gain advantage on initiative rolls and Dexterity saving throws against area effects. |  
| 17th | **Living Lightning** – Once per long rest, you can move up to your full speed in a blink, striking all creatures in your path. |  

---

### **Way of the Hollow Step**  
*"The less they see you, the more power you have."*  

#### **Features & Playstyle**  
- **Masters of light distortion, stepping through urban shadows and hiding in plain sight.**  
- Uses **blinding speed, disappearing strikes, and spatial anomalies** in combat.  
- Common among **street assassins, A.S.T.R.A.L. hunters, and urban phantoms.**  

#### **Monastic Abilities**  
| Level | Feature |  
|-------|---------|  
| 3rd | **Blink Step** – As a reaction, when attacked, you can teleport 10 feet away instead of taking damage. |  
| 6th | **Liminal Shift** – You can move through walls and obstacles as difficult terrain. |  
| 11th | **Phantom Barrage** – Once per short rest, you can attack an enemy from multiple angles, making two strikes against them in the same turn. |  
| 17th | **Erased Presence** – Once per long rest, you can become untargetable by all creatures for 1 minute. You can still attack, but no enemy can perceive you. |  

---

### **Way of the Ruinwalker**  
*"The city is breaking. I am its hammer."*  

#### **Features & Playstyle**  
- **Wields entropy, collapse, and destruction as a weapon.**  
- Excels at **crushing structures, breaking enemies, and decaying obstacles.**  
- Common among **wasteland monks, ruin mystics, and demolition experts.**  

#### **Monastic Abilities**  
| Level | Feature |  
|-------|---------|  
| 3rd | **Fists of Collapse** – Your unarmed strikes ignore damage resistance against constructs and objects. |  
| 6th | **Breaking Touch** – You can use your action to weaken an object, making it vulnerable to all damage for 1 minute. |  
| 11th | **Crack the Foundation** – Once per short rest, you can strike a surface, causing a **10-foot radius collapse**, forcing creatures inside to make a Dexterity saving throw or fall prone. |  
| 17th | **Entropic Strike** – Once per long rest, you can touch a target and force them to make a Constitution saving throw. On a failure, they begin **crumbling into dust** over the next minute. |  

---

### **Way of the Soundless**  
*"Words are wasted. Sound is a weapon."*  

#### **Features & Playstyle**  
- **Masters of absolute silence, fighting in complete stillness.**  
- Uses **vibration-based strikes, subsonic control, and sound-nullifying combat.**  
- Common among **corporate spies, underground killers, and the unseen enforcers.**  

\page

#### **Monastic Abilities**  
| Level | Feature |  
|-------|---------|  
| 3rd | **Quiet Killer** – Your attacks make no sound. Creatures have disadvantage on Perception checks to detect you. |  
| 6th | **Echo Suppression** – You can silence a 10-foot radius around you for 1 minute, nullifying verbal spellcasting inside it. |  
| 11th | **Subsonic Impact** – Once per short rest, you can strike an enemy with a force that vibrates through their body, preventing them from speaking or casting spells for 1 minute. |  
| 17th | **Resonant Death** – Once per long rest, you can strike a creature with a vibration that builds within them. If they do not receive magical healing within 1 minute, they take **10d10 thunder damage.** |  

---

### **Way of the Fractured Mind (Paradox Walker & Temporal Instability)**  
*"I have already seen this battle. And I have already won."*  

#### **Features & Playstyle**  
- **Manipulates reality fractures, seeing alternate possibilities before they unfold.**  
- Uses **precognition, temporal shifts, and flickering movements** in combat.  
- Common among **anomaly survivors, time-lost wanderers, and those who see too much.**  

#### **Monastic Abilities**  
| Level | Feature |  
|-------|---------|  
| 3rd | **Temporal Reflexes** – Gain advantage on initiative rolls. Once per long rest, you can reroll a failed Dexterity saving throw by momentarily stepping into an alternate timeline. |  
| 6th | **Split Awareness** – You can glimpse a few seconds into the future. Once per short rest, when an enemy targets you with an attack, you can force them to reroll it. |  
| 11th | **Dimensional Slip** – When you use Step of the Wind, you can teleport up to 15 feet instead of moving normally. |  
| 17th | **Fractured Time** – Once per long rest, you can briefly step outside of time, allowing you to take an extra turn immediately after your current one. |  

---

### **Way of the Iron Circuit (Cybernetic Monk & Technokinetic Mastery)**  
*"The body is weak. The machine is strong."*  

#### **Features & Playstyle**  
- **Enhances ki through cybernetic implants and energy manipulation.**  
- Wields **electric strikes, neural acceleration, and kinetic energy surges.**  
- Common among **corporate soldiers, rogue cyborg monks, and A.S.T.R.A.L. experiments.**  

#### **Monastic Abilities**  
| Level | Feature |  
|-------|---------|  
| 3rd | **Neural Surge** – Your reaction speed is enhanced. Gain resistance to mind-affecting effects and can add your Wisdom modifier to initiative rolls. |  
| 6th | **Electrostrike** – Your unarmed strikes deal additional lightning damage equal to your Wisdom modifier. Once per short rest, you can stun an enemy with a pulse of electricity. |  
| 11th | **Kinetic Overload** – When you land a critical hit, you can release a burst of stored energy, forcing all creatures within 10 feet to make a Strength saving throw or be knocked prone. |  
| 17th | **Cybernetic Apex** – Once per long rest, you can activate a state of perfect synchronization, doubling your movement speed and gaining advantage on all attack rolls for 1 minute. |  

---

### **Way of the Hollow Spirit (Echoes of the Departed & Spectral Combat)**  
*"The dead are never silent. And I listen."*  

#### **Features & Playstyle**  
- **Channels spectral echoes, fighting alongside lingering spirits.**  
- Uses **phasing movement, spectral shielding, and wraith-like abilities.**  
- Common among **forgotten monks, urban mediums, and haunted warriors.**  

#### **Monastic Abilities**  
| Level | Feature |  
|-------|---------|  
| 3rd | **Ghost Step** – As a reaction when attacked, you can briefly phase, granting you resistance to non-magical attacks until the end of your turn. |  
| 6th | **Spectral Defense** – While moving, you become harder to hit. If you move at least 10 feet on your turn, attack rolls against you have disadvantage until the start of your next turn. |  
| 11th | **Wraith Form** – Once per short rest, you can assume an incorporeal form for 1 minute. While in this state, you can move through solid objects and gain resistance to all damage except force and psychic. |  
| 17th | **Ancestral Manifestation** – Once per long rest, you can call forth spectral echoes to fight alongside you for 1 minute. These spirits grant you a bonus attack each turn and impose disadvantage on enemy attacks against you. |

- Take a monofilament staff and an armored bodysuit for maximum efficiency.

## **Paladin**  
*Corporate Crusader | Paranormal Knight | Oathbound Enforcer | Reality Warden*  

> *"Faith isn’t in gods—it’s in power, in authority, in the unshakable will to shape the world."*  
> — **Commander Aven Voss, Iron Pact**  

### **Thematic Overview**  
Paladins in Concord City are not just warriors of faith—they are **enforcers of ideology, keepers of ancient oaths, and wielders of reality-binding power**. Some swear allegiance to **corporations, noble houses, or forgotten entities**, while others are **rogue zealots** pursuing their own brand of justice. Their power comes not from deities, but from **absolute conviction, paranormal attunement, or secret doctrines**.
- Paladins serve as **champions of law, crusaders of forgotten truths, or elite corporate enforcers**.  
- Some act as **agents of Thaumatech, A.S.T.R.A.L., or private militaries**.  
- Others walk the path of **anarchists, outcasts, or rogue knights** upholding their own code.  
- Their oaths bind them to a **cause, a purpose, or a hidden truth only they understand**.  

### **Creating a Paladin**  
- Who or what do you serve? A corporation, a cause, or something supernatural?  
- Did you swear your oath willingly, or was it forced upon you?  
- How do you enforce your beliefs—through justice, order, or sheer force?  

## **Class Features**  
As a **Paladin**, you gain the following class features.

### **Hit Points**  
- **Hit Dice:** *1d10 per Paladin level*  
- **Hit Points at 1st Level:** *10 + Constitution modifier*  
- **Hit Points at Higher Levels:** *1d10 (or 6) + Constitution modifier per level after 1st*  

### **Proficiencies**  
- **Armor:** *All armor, shields*  
- **Weapons:** *Simple weapons, martial weapons*  
- **Tools:** *None*  
- **Saving Throws:** *Wisdom, Charisma*  
- **Skills:** *Choose two from Athletics, Insight, Intimidation, Medicine, Persuasion, and Religion*  

### **Equipment**  
You start with the following equipment, in addition to any granted by your background:  
- *(a)* a tactical longsword or *(b)* a plasma hammer  
- *(a)* a heavy pistol with 10 rounds or *(b)* a combat shield  
- *(a)* a corporate-issued badge or *(b)* a knightly insignia  
- A set of encrypted mission dossiers or an ancient relic

\page
## **Class Abilities**  
### **Divine Sense (Level 1)**  
You can detect **paranormal presences, reality distortions, or ideological corruption** nearby.

### **Lay on Hands (Level 1)**  
You can restore hit points by channeling your **inner conviction or anomalous energy**, with a pool of **5 HP per Paladin level**.

### **Fighting Style (Level 2)**  
Choose a fighting style that reflects your training and beliefs.
- **Dueling:** +2 to damage while wielding a one-handed weapon.  
- **Defense:** +1 AC while wearing armor.  
- **Great Weapon Fighting:** Reroll 1s and 2s on melee weapon damage.  
- **Protection:** Use your shield to impose disadvantage on attacks.  

### **Divine Smite (Level 2)**  
You can channel your **ideological will or supernatural energy** into a strike, dealing **radiant or necrotic damage**.


## **Subclasses: Sacred Oaths**  
At **3rd level**, you swear an oath that defines your role in the world.

In Concord City, paladins are not holy knights but enforcers of power, ideology, and order. Whether aligned with corporations, rebellion, monarchy, or anomaly containment, these warriors uphold their oaths with unwavering commitment.


### **Oath of Profit**
*“Wealth is power, and power is justice.”*

#### **Tenets of Profit**
- **Maximize Returns** – Every action should generate measurable value.
- **Brand Loyalty** – Uphold the interests of your corporate benefactors.
- **Monetize Justice** – Righteousness is defined by the highest bidder.
- **Eliminate Competition** – Remove threats to the corporate status quo.

#### **Oath Spells**
| Level | Spells |
|-------|--------|
| 3rd | Corporate Mandate, Data Scan |
| 5th | Market Suggestion, Lockdown Protocol |
| 9th | Signal Jam, Privacy Protocol |
| 13th | Executive Privilege, Corporate Mass Production |
| 17th | Hostile Acquisition, Containment Barrier |

#### **Channel Divinity**
- **Hostile Takeover** – As an action, force a creature to make a Wisdom saving throw. On a failure, they obey your verbal commands for 1 minute (as if under the *Market Suggestion* spell).
- **Market Stability** – You create a 30-foot aura where allies gain temporary HP equal to your Charisma modifier whenever they make a financial or persuasion-based transaction.

---

### **Oath of Resistance**
*“We stand, we fight, we never kneel.”*

#### **Tenets of Resistance**
- **Defy Tyranny** – Challenge any system that oppresses the weak.
- **No Chains Shall Bind** – No law or corporate edict can dictate your fate.
- **Strength in Unity** – The cause survives only if we protect one another.
- **Die on Your Feet** – Never surrender to those who hoard power.

#### **Oath Spells**
| Level | Spells |
|-------|--------|
| 3rd | Sonic Suppression, Safehouse Protocol |
| 5th | Infrastructure Collapse, Ghost Transit |
| 9th | Overclocked Reflexes, Encrypted Barrier |
| 13th | Untethered Motion, Executive Privilege |
| 17th | Corporate Crackdown, Containment Barrier |

#### **Channel Divinity**
- **Rally the Masses** – Inspire up to six creatures within 30 feet, granting them advantage on attack rolls and saving throws against being charmed or frightened for 1 minute.
- **Saboteur’s Strike** – When you hit a creature or object, you can deal bonus force damage equal to twice your paladin level and disable one function (e.g., a weapon, a cybernetic implant, or a security system) for 1 minute.

---

### **Oath of Allegiance**
*“Our duty is eternal, our loyalty unbroken.”*

#### **Tenets of Allegiance**
- **Serve the Sovereign** – The ruler is the heart of the city; you are the sword and shield.
- **Honor Above All** – Your word is your bond, and betrayal is the gravest sin.
- **Strength Through Order** – A stable society requires a structured hierarchy.
- **Defend the Legacy** – The past must be preserved to guide the future.

\page

#### **Oath Spells**
| Level | Spells |
|-------|--------|
| 3rd | Challenge of Rank, Royal Decree |
| 5th | Lockdown Protocol, Warding Bond |
| 9th | Imperial Radiance, Bureaucratic Override |
| 13th | Sentinel of Order, Historical Rectification |
| 17th | Divine Enforcement, Royal Mandate |

#### **Channel Divinity**
- **Imperial Edict** – As an action, force up to three creatures to make a Charisma saving throw. On a failure, they cannot attack you or your allies for 1 minute unless directly provoked.
- **Royal Decree** – You can grant temporary HP to all allies within 30 feet equal to twice your Charisma modifier and remove one status effect from each affected ally.

---

### **Oath of Protection**
*“To Secure, To Contain, To Protect.”*

#### **Tenets of Protection**
- **Contain the Unknown** – Anomalies must be neutralized before they endanger society.
- **Preserve Order** – Reality must remain stable, and threats must be controlled.
- **Shield the Innocent** – Protect those who cannot defend themselves from the unseen.
- **Secrecy is Security** – The public does not need to know what lurks in the dark.

#### **Oath Spells**
| Level | Spells |
|-------|--------|
| 3rd | Detect Anomaly, Protection from Corruption |
| 5th | Zone of Truth, Contain Threat |
| 9th | Dispel Anomaly, Countermeasure |

| 17th | Reality Lockdown, Total Erasure |

#### **Channel Divinity**
- **Nullification Field** – As an action, create a 10-foot aura for 1 minute where spells and supernatural effects within the area are negated unless they succeed on a spellcasting ability check against your spell save DC.
- **Emergency Containment** – As an action, bind a creature or anomaly in glowing energy for 1 minute, preventing it from teleporting or phasing through matter. It must succeed on a Strength saving throw to break free.

---

### **Oath of the Enforcer**
*"Law is not about justice. It is about control."*  

#### **Tenets of the Enforcer**
- **Law is Absolute** – The law must be upheld, regardless of morality.  
- **No Exceptions** – Mercy is a weakness that leads to disorder.  
- **The Strongest Hand** – Power belongs to those who can wield it effectively.  
- **Punish the Unruly** – Dissent must be silenced before it spreads.  

#### **Oath Spells**

#### **Channel Divinity**  
- **Impose Order** – As an action, force up to three creatures within 30 feet to make a Wisdom saving throw. On a failure, they are frightened of you for 1 minute.  
- **Judgment Strike** – When you hit a creature, you can mark them as a criminal. They take additional psychic damage equal to twice your Paladin level and have disadvantage on saving throws against your abilities for 1 minute.  

---

### **Oath of the Forsaken**
*"I am the line between their world and ours."*  

#### **Tenets of the Forsaken**
- **Sacrifice for Order** – To protect the world, you must be willing to lose yourself.  
- **Contain the Unknowable** – The less people know, the safer they are.  
- **Eradicate the Unnatural** – No mercy for what does not belong.  
- **Walk Alone** – This duty is yours alone, and no one will thank you for it.  

#### **Oath Spells**  
| Level | Spells |  
|-------|--------|  
| 3rd | Detect Anomaly, Contain Threat |  
| 5th | Nullify Presence, Spectral Shackles |  
| 9th | Dispel Anomaly, Banished Echo |  
| 13th | Erase Entity, Planar Isolation |  
| 17th | Total Erasure, Astral Seal |

\page

#### **Channel Divinity**  
- **Suppress the Unseen** – As an action, you force any invisible or extraplanar creature within 30 feet to become visible and lose their resistances for 1 minute.  
- **Sever the Connection** – When you strike a creature, you can cut off their connection to their power source, preventing them from using spellcasting or supernatural abilities for 1 minute.  

---

### **Oath of the Blackguard**
*"I did what needed to be done. The gods never answered."*  

#### **Tenets of the Blackguard**
- **Faith is a Lie** – No divine hand will save you. Take what you need.  
- **Survival Above All** – The weak die. The strong endure.  
- **Vengeance is Justice** – If the world abandoned you, then burn it down.  
- **No Chains, No Masters** – Serve no god, no law, no corporation.  

#### **Oath Spells**  
| Level | Spells |  
|-------|--------|  
| 3rd | Siphon Strength, Dark Mandate |  
| 5th | Corrupt Authority, Phantom Chains |  
| 9th | Banish Radiance, Hunger of the Forgotten |  
| 13th | Sinister Pact, Cloak of Shadows |  
| 17th | Absolute Corruption, Death’s Promise |  

#### **Channel Divinity**  
- **Dark Oath** – Once per long rest, you can make a vow of vengeance against a target. For the next 10 minutes, all attacks against them have advantage, and they cannot regain HP.  
- **Void Strike** – Your attack is infused with unnatural force. On a hit, the target must succeed on a Constitution saving throw or become unable to regain HP for 1 hour.  

---

### **Oath of the Digital Templar**
*"Information is the only truth. I protect the purity of data."*  

#### **Tenets of the Digital Templar**
- **Truth in Data** – All lies are temporary. The truth is recorded forever.  
- **Purify the Corrupt** – Corruption in the network must be expunged.  
- **No Privacy in Judgment** – If your actions are righteous, you have nothing to hide.  
- **Defend the Archive** – Knowledge is the only lasting power.  

#### **Oath Spells**  
| Level | Spells |  
|-------|--------|  
| 3rd | Data Scan, Signal Encryption |  
| 5th | Firewall, Nullify Presence |  
| 9th | Trace Connection, Overclocked Reflexes |  
| 13th | Digital Exorcism, Memory Rewrite |  
| 17th | Absolute Surveillance, Reality Firewall |  

#### **Channel Divinity**  
- **Data Lockdown** – As an action, you prevent any creature within 60 feet from speaking falsehoods, disguising themselves, or hiding their identity for 1 minute.  
- **Excommunicate Virus** – You may force a machine or cybernetic being to make a Wisdom saving throw. On a failure, they shut down for 1 minute.  

---

### **Oath of the Hollow**  
*"I am the voice of the lost, the guardian of the erased."*  

#### **Tenets of the Hollow**
- **Erase, Protect, Forget** – Some things must be lost to preserve the whole.  
- **Guard the Silent** – The most dangerous knowledge is that which whispers from the void.  
- **Witness the End** – You are the last record of what should not be known.  
- **No Name, No Face** – To protect the city, you must not exist.  

#### **Oath Spells**  
| Level | Spells |  
|-------|--------|  
| 3rd | Ghost Transit, Whispered Oath |  
| 5th | Memory Suppression, Cloak of Anonymity |  
| 9th | Severed Connection, Banished Echo |  
| 13th | Echo of the Lost, Planar Isolation |  
| 17th | Reality Lockdown, Total Erasure |  

#### **Channel Divinity**  
- **Unseen Guardian** – As a reaction, you can become completely undetectable for 1 minute, even to magical means.  
- **Silence the Past** – Force a target to make a Wisdom saving throw. On failure, they forget the last hour of their memory.  

\page

### **Oath of the Blood Pact**  
*"A deal is a deal. Even the gods obey the contract."*  

#### **Tenets of the Blood Pact**
- **The Contract is Everything** – There are no loopholes. There is no escape.  
- **Power is Earned** – If you did not pay for it, you do not deserve it.  
- **The Debt is Paid** – No promise is broken. No betrayal is forgotten.  
- **Blood Seals All** – The strongest oaths are written in the veins.  

#### **Oath Spells**  
| Level | Spells |  
|-------|--------|  
| 3rd | Marked for Collection, Compliance Protocol |  
| 5th | Blood Price, Hostile Acquisition |  
| 9th | Pact Brand, Enforce Contract |  
| 13th | Unbreakable Covenant, Cloak of Debt |  
| 17th | Ultimate Arbitration, Divine Collateral |  

#### **Channel Divinity**  
- **Seal the Pact** – You can enforce an agreement magically. A creature that tries to break it suffers radiant damage equal to half its HP.  
- **Blood Binding** – You mark a creature. Until you release them, they suffer disadvantage on all rolls against you.  


---

## **Multiclassing**  
If your campaign allows multiclassing, use the following rules for a **Paladin** multiclass character.  

### **Ability Score Minimums**  
- Strength 13, Charisma 13  

### **Proficiencies Gained**  
- Light armor, medium armor, shields, simple weapons, martial weapons  


## **Quick Build**  
You can make a **Paladin** quickly by following these suggestions:  
- Choose **Human or Tiefling** for a thematic fit.  
- Pick the **Corporate Enforcer** or **Exiled Knight** background.  
- Prioritize **Strength and Charisma**.  
- Take a tactical longsword and combat shield for maximum efficiency.

## **Ranger**  
*Urban Tracker | Paranormal Hunter | Corporate Scout | Wilderness Survivor*  

> *"The city has a pulse, a rhythm. If you listen, you’ll know where to strike."*  
> — **Léna Duval, The Pariahs**  

### **Thematic Overview**  
Rangers in Concord City are not bound to forests or wildlands—they are **trackers, survivalists, and specialists in navigating the treacherous landscapes of urban sprawl and paranormal zones**. Some are trained by **corporate security forces**, others work **for underground movements**, and some are lone wanderers protecting forgotten ruins. Their expertise lets them hunt **paranormal creatures, criminals, or anomalies** with ruthless efficiency.
- Rangers are **adaptive warriors, skilled in tracking, survival, and specialized combat**.  
- Some serve as **A.S.T.R.A.L. operatives**, hunting reality-warping threats.  
- Others work as **urban explorers, black-market smugglers, or freelance investigators**.  
- They are attuned to the **unnatural elements of the world, sensing disturbances beyond normal perception**.  

### **Creating a Ranger**  
- Do you serve a higher cause, or are you a rogue operating on your own terms?  
- Are you a trained corporate operative, or did you learn survival the hard way?  
- What threats do you hunt—corporate agents, supernatural creatures, or something worse?  

---

## **Class Features**  
As a **Ranger**, you gain the following class features.

### **Hit Points**  
- **Hit Dice:** *1d10 per Ranger level*  
- **Hit Points at 1st Level:** *10 + Constitution modifier*  
- **Hit Points at Higher Levels:** *1d10 (or 6) + Constitution modifier per level after 1st*  

### **Proficiencies**  
- **Armor:** *Light armor, medium armor, shields*  
- **Weapons:** *Simple weapons, martial weapons*  
- **Tools:** *Choose one: hacker’s kit, survival gear, or demolitions kit*  
- **Saving Throws:** *Strength, Dexterity*  
- **Skills:** *Choose three from Acrobatics, Athletics, Insight, Investigation, Nature, Perception, Stealth, and Survival*  

### **Equipment**  
You start with the following equipment, in addition to any granted by your background:  
- *(a)* a long-range rifle and 20 rounds or *(b)* two silenced handguns  
- *(a)* a tactical blade or *(b)* a collapsible baton  
- *(a)* an urban survival pack or *(b)* a data-extraction kit  
- A high-tech scanner or an encrypted commlink  

---

| 19th | +6 | Ability Score Improvement | 4 |  
| 20th | +6 | Foe Slayer | 4 |  

---

\page

## **Class Abilities**  
### **Favored Enemy (Level 1)**  
You have trained to hunt specific threats, such as **corporate enforcers, rogue paranormals, or extradimensional anomalies**. You gain advantage on tracking and intelligence checks related to your chosen enemy.

### **Natural Explorer (Level 1)**  
Instead of wild terrains, you specialize in navigating and surviving within **urban ruins, paranormal zones, or high-tech environments**.

### **Fighting Style (Level 2)**  
Choose a fighting style that reflects your training:
- **Marksman:** +2 to attack rolls with ranged weapons.  
- **Brawler:** +1 AC and unarmed strikes deal 1d6 damage.  
- **Dual-Wielding:** When two-weapon fighting, you add your ability modifier to the second attack.  
- **Hunter’s Precision:** Your attacks score a critical hit on a 19-20.  

### **Primeval Awareness (Level 3)**  
By expending a spell slot, you can detect the presence of **paranormal entities, reality distortions, or supernatural creatures** within a mile.

---

## **Subclasses: Ranger Archetypes**  
At **3rd level**, you choose a Ranger Archetype that defines your hunting style.


---

### **The Gridrunner**  
*"If you exist in the system, I can find you."*  

#### **Features & Playstyle**  
- **Masters of surveillance, hacking, and digital forensics.**  
- Uses **drones, data trails, and augmented tracking to hunt their prey.**  
- Common among **corporate security agents, private detectives, and bounty hunters.**  

#### **Archetype Abilities**  
| Level | Feature |  
|-------|---------|  
| 3rd | **Network Trace** – Gain proficiency in Investigation. You can scan digital footprints to track a target’s movement through the city. |  
| 7th | **Surveillance Mastery** – Gain advantage on Perception checks to detect creatures using cameras, sensors, or digital tracking. |  
| 11th | **Augmented Hunt** – Once per short rest, you can mark a target. While marked, you always know their direction and they cannot hide from electronic surveillance. |  
| 15th | **Omnipresent Stalker** – You can predict a target’s movements so precisely that they have disadvantage on attempts to escape or deceive you. |  

---

### **The Rustborn**  
*"The city crumbles, but I endure."*  

#### **Features & Playstyle**  
- **Thrives in abandoned, decaying, and toxic environments.**  
- Excels at **scavenging, improvised survival, and resisting urban decay.**  
- Common among **wasteland rangers, ruin explorers, and scavenger warriors.**  

#### **Archetype Abilities**  
| Level | Feature |  
|-------|---------|  
| 3rd | **Urban Resilience** – Gain resistance to poison and immunity to disease. You can subsist on contaminated food and water without harm. |  
| 7th | **Scrap Weaponry** – You can craft makeshift weapons from debris, allowing you to deal extra damage with scavenged items. |  
| 11th | **Adaptive Camouflage** – Gain advantage on Stealth checks when in ruined, abandoned, or industrial areas. |  
| 15th | **Survivor’s Endurance** – When reduced to 0 HP, you can drop to 1 HP instead once per long rest. |  

---

### **The Etherstalker**  
*"Nothing escapes me. Not even between realities."*  

#### **Features & Playstyle**  
- **Masters of tracking and fighting creatures that phase between worlds.**  
- Uses **dimensional disruption, reality anchoring, and spectral weaponry.**  
- Common among **A.S.T.R.A.L. operatives, ghost hunters, and interplanar bounty trackers.**  

\page

#### **Archetype Abilities**  
| Level | Feature |  
|-------|---------|  
| 3rd | **Phase Tracker** – You can sense nearby entities that are invisible, phased, or not fully in this reality. |  
| 7th | **Dimensional Anchor** – When you hit a creature, you can force it to stay in this plane for 1 minute, preventing teleportation or phasing. |  
| 11th | **Void Strikes** – Your attacks ignore resistances and immunities against phased, ethereal, or extraplanar beings. |  
| 15th | **Step Between Worlds** – Once per long rest, you can slip partially out of phase, becoming resistant to all damage except force. |  

---

### **The Riot Gunner**  
*"One shot is all I need."*  

#### **Features & Playstyle**  
- **Excels at urban warfare, close-quarters marksmanship, and suppressing enemies.**  
- Uses **high-speed combat tactics and precision shooting.**  
- Common among **corporate snipers, riot police, and paramilitary operatives.**  

#### **Archetype Abilities**  
| Level | Feature |  
|-------|---------|  
| 3rd | **Suppressive Fire** – When you hit a creature with a ranged attack, they have disadvantage on their next attack. |  
| 7th | **Tactical Repositioning** – When you use the Dash action, you can make a ranged attack as a bonus action. |  
| 11th | **Armor Piercer** – Your ranged attacks ignore half and three-quarters cover. |  
| 15th | **Killing Floor** – Once per long rest, when you reduce a creature to 0 HP, all enemies within 10 feet of the target must make a Wisdom saving throw or become frightened for 1 minute. |  

---

### **The Street Rat**  
*"They own the towers. We own the streets."*  

#### **Features & Playstyle**  
- **Masters of navigating urban environments, blending into crowds, and using deception in combat.**  
- Excels at **trickery, dirty fighting, and rapid escape.**  
- Common among **gang scouts, thieves, and underground couriers.**  

#### **Archetype Abilities**  
| Level | Feature |  
|-------|---------|  
| 3rd | **Blend In** – Gain proficiency in Deception. When in a crowd, you can use a bonus action to Hide. |  
| 7th | **Quick Hands** – You can draw or stow a weapon and make an attack as part of the same action. |  
| 11th | **Slippery Target** – When an enemy attacks you, you can use your reaction to impose disadvantage on the attack. |  
| 15th | **Urban Ghost** – Once per long rest, you can disappear into a crowd, becoming undetectable for 1 minute. |  

---

### **The Augmented Tracker**  
*"My body is an upgrade. My prey has no escape."*  

#### **Features & Playstyle**  
- **Masters of cybernetic enhancements for enhanced hunting.**  
- Uses **mechanical precision, augmented perception, and enhanced reflexes.**  
- Common among **corporate super-soldiers, cybernetic hunters, and enhanced mercenaries.**  

#### **Archetype Abilities**  
| Level | Feature |  
|-------|---------|  
| 3rd | **Augmented Vision** – You gain darkvision up to 120 feet and advantage on Perception checks using sight. |  
| 7th | **Cybernetic Reflexes** – Gain a +2 bonus to initiative and advantage on Dexterity saving throws. |  
| 11th | **Neural Targeting** – Once per short rest, you can analyze a target, allowing your next attack against them to automatically hit. |  
| 15th | **Overclocked Pursuit** – Once per long rest, you can enter a heightened state for 1 minute, doubling your speed and granting you an additional reaction each round. |  

---

### **Urban Ghost**  
*"The city is my hunting ground. I am never seen, only felt."*  

#### **Features & Playstyle**  
- **Thrives in urban environments, moving unseen and striking with precision.**  
- Specializes in **stealth, assassination, and blending into cityscapes.**  
- Common among **rogue operatives, street hunters, and corporate spies.**  

#### **Archetype Abilities**

| 11th | **Shadow Meld** – After making an attack, you can use a bonus action to turn invisible until the start of your next turn. |  
| 15th | **Phantom Stalker** – You cannot be detected by mundane or magical means unless you choose to reveal yourself. |

*"Supernatural or not, everything leaves a trail."*

- **Trains to track, identify, and neutralize supernatural threats.**  
- Wields **paranormal senses, banishment strikes, and reality-warping resistance.**  
- Common among **A.S.T.R.A.L. operatives, cryptid hunters, and rogue anomaly specialists.**

| 7th | **Warded Mind** – Gain resistance to mind-affecting effects and advantage on saving throws against fear and charm. |  
| 11th | **Banishment Strike** – Once per short rest, when you strike a supernatural entity, you can force it to make a Charisma saving throw or be temporarily exiled from reality. |  
| 15th | **Unshakable Tracker** – You always know the direction of any marked target, even through teleportation or planar shifts. |  

---

### **Corporate Retainer**  
*"I don’t work for free. You get what you pay for."*  

#### **Features & Playstyle**

- Common among **security contractors, mercenaries, and corporate black ops units.**

| 11th | **Suppression Fire** – When you hit a target with a ranged attack, they must make a Wisdom saving throw or be unable to take reactions until your next turn. |  
| 15th | **Unyielding Pursuer** – You are immune to being charmed or frightened. You also ignore movement penalties while chasing a marked target. |  

---

### **Deadeye Sniper**  
*"One shot. One kill. That’s the job."*  

#### **Features & Playstyle**  
- **Specializes in long-range marksmanship and precision eliminations.**  
- Uses **stealth, scope-assisted targeting, and deadly precision shots.**  
- Common among **corporate assassins, military sharpshooters, and rogue snipers.**  

#### **Archetype Abilities**

|-------|---------|  
| 3rd | **Scoped Focus** – Gain proficiency with sniper rifles. If you take an entire turn aiming without moving, your next shot automatically lands as a critical hit. |  
| 7th | **Ghost Positioning** – After firing a ranged attack, you can move up to half your speed without provoking opportunity attacks. |  
| 11th | **Lethal Precision** – When you make a ranged attack at least 60 feet away, you can add your Intelligence modifier to the damage roll. |  
| 15th | **Assassination Protocol** – Once per long rest, if you hit a creature with a ranged attack, you can force them to make a Constitution saving throw. On failure, they drop to 0 HP instantly. |

- Take a long-range rifle and an urban survival pack for maximum effectiveness.

## **Rogue**  
*Corporate Spy | Paranormal Infiltrator | Master Thief | Shadow Operative*  

> *"Loyalty is expensive. Secrets are priceless."*  
> — **Cipher-9, Obscura**  

### **Thematic Overview**  
Rogues in Concord City are masters of deception, infiltration, and precision. They **thrive in the underbelly of society, within corporate espionage divisions, or as lone operatives playing every side**. Some use **technology to hack security grids**, others rely on **paranormal attunement to become ghosts in the system**. Whether working for crime syndicates, corporations, or themselves, rogues shape the flow of information and power.
- Rogues are **stealthy operatives, hackers, thieves, and assassins**.  
- Some work as **black-market data couriers, corporate spies, or political saboteurs**.  
- Others use **paranormal talents to vanish, manipulate shadows, or bend probability**.  
- Every rogue has a **code**, whether it's personal survival, anarchy, or corporate loyalty.  

### **Creating a Rogue**  
- Do you steal for wealth, knowledge, or survival?  
- Are you a trained infiltrator, or did you learn the trade on the streets?  
- Who do you serve—yourself, a faction, or something unknown?  

---

## **Class Features**  
As a **Rogue**, you gain the following class features.

### **Hit Points**  
- **Hit Dice:** *1d8 per Rogue level*  
- **Hit Points at 1st Level:** *8 + Constitution modifier*  
- **Hit Points at Higher Levels:** *1d8 (or 5) + Constitution modifier per level after 1st*  

### **Proficiencies**  
- **Armor:** *Light armor*  
- **Weapons:** *Simple weapons, hand crossbows, longswords, rapiers, short swords*  
- **Tools:** *Thieves’ tools, one other of your choice (hacker’s kit, forgery tools, etc.)*  
- **Saving Throws:** *Dexterity, Intelligence*  
- **Skills:** *Choose four from Acrobatics, Athletics, Deception, Insight, Intimidation, Investigation, Perception, Persuasion, Sleight of Hand, and Stealth*  

### **Equipment**  
You start with the following equipment, in addition to any granted by your background:  
- *(a)* a silenced pistol and 10 rounds or *(b)* a pair of daggers  
- *(a)* a stealth suit or *(b)* an urban tactical jacket  
- *(a)* a set of lockpicks or *(b)* a hacking deck  
- An encrypted communicator or a counterfeit ID  

---

| 20th | +6 | Stroke of Luck | 10d6 |

\page

## **Class Abilities**  
### **Sneak Attack (Level 1)**  
You know how to exploit weaknesses in enemies. Once per turn, when you hit with an attack **while having advantage or when an ally is within 5 feet of the target**, you deal extra damage based on your **Sneak Attack dice**.

### **Cunning Action (Level 2)**  
You can take the **Dash, Disengage, or Hide action** as a bonus action on your turn.

### **Uncanny Dodge (Level 5)**  
When an attacker you can see hits you with an attack, you can use your reaction to halve the damage.

---

## **Subclasses: Roguish Archetypes**  
At **3rd level**, you choose a Roguish Archetype that defines your approach to subterfuge.

---

### **Ghost Operative**  
*"No alarms. No witnesses. No evidence."*  

#### **Features & Playstyle**  
- **Masters of espionage, cyber-infiltration, and corporate sabotage.**  
- Uses **hacking, stealth, and surveillance disruption** to operate unseen.  
- Common among **corporate spies, underground hackers, and intelligence agents.**  

#### **Archetype Abilities**  
| Level | Feature |  
|-------|---------|  
| 3rd | **Digital Infiltrator** – Gain advantage on hacking attempts and rolls made to bypass security systems. |  
| 9th | **Erased Presence** – Surveillance cameras and tracking systems automatically fail to detect you. You do not leave a digital footprint. |  
| 13th | **Neural Suppression** – Once per long rest, you can force an enemy to make an Intelligence saving throw. On failure, they forget the last minute of events. |  
| 17th | **Master of Shadows** – You are permanently under the effects of *Nondetection*, and even supernatural tracking methods struggle to locate you. |  

---

### **Phantom Veil**  
*"I am here. I am gone. You never saw me."*  

#### **Features & Playstyle**  
- **Blends illusion, supernatural movement, and reality manipulation into stealth.**  
- Uses **shifting phases, dim light camouflage, and teleportation tricks.**  
- Common among **mystic infiltrators, void-dancers, and urban legends.**  

#### **Archetype Abilities**  
| Level | Feature |  
|-------|---------|  
| 3rd | **Echo Step** – Once per short rest, you can teleport up to 30 feet as a bonus action. |  
| 9th | **Ethereal Infiltrator** – You can phase through thin walls or barriers, moving through solid matter up to 5 feet thick. |  
| 13th | **Veil Cloak** – While in dim light or darkness, you cannot be targeted by attacks or spells unless the attacker has true sight. |  
| 17th | **Beyond the Veil** – You become partially intangible. For 1 minute per long rest, non-magical attacks pass through you, dealing only half damage. |  

---

### **Black Market Kingpin**  
*"Every secret has a price. And I set the market."*  

#### **Features & Playstyle**  
- **Masters of information, trade secrets, and underground deals.**  
- Wields **bribery, persuasion, and financial leverage as weapons.**  
- Common among **crime lords, shadow brokers, and economic manipulators.**  

#### **Archetype Abilities**  
| Level | Feature |  
|-------|---------|  
| 3rd | **Insider Connections** – Gain access to exclusive black-market resources. You can procure rare items with ease. |  
| 9th | **Information Broker** – Gain advantage on rolls to gather rumors, blackmail material, or corporate secrets. |  
| 13th | **Bribe the System** – Once per short rest, when you fail a Persuasion or Deception check, you can reroll it by offering a bribe. |  
| 17th | **Untouchable** – You always have an escape plan. Once per long rest, when caught in an unwinnable situation, you can automatically vanish, leaving behind no trace of your presence. |  

---

### **Deadeye Sniper**  
*"One shot. One ghost. No loose ends."*  

#### **Features & Playstyle**  
- **Masters of extreme long-range assassinations.**  
- Uses **stealth, precision marksmanship, and patience to eliminate targets.**  
- Common among **corporate assassins, military snipers, and rogue contract killers.**  

\page

#### **Archetype Abilities**  
| Level | Feature |  
|-------|---------|  
| 3rd | **Scoped Kill** – If you aim at a target for an entire turn without moving, your next ranged attack automatically scores a critical hit if it lands. |  
| 9th | **Ghost Positioning** – When you fire a ranged attack, you can move up to half your speed without provoking opportunity attacks. |  
| 13th | **Lethal Precision** – Your ranged weapon attacks deal additional damage equal to your Intelligence modifier. |  
| 17th | **Perfect Shot** – Once per long rest, when you hit a creature with a ranged attack, you can force them to make a Constitution saving throw. On failure, they drop to 0 HP instantly. |  

---

### **Neural Phantom**  
*"I don't steal your credits. I steal your mind."*  

#### **Features & Playstyle**  
- **Masters of hacking thoughts, manipulating memories, and rewiring minds.**  
- Uses **mental infiltration, forced illusions, and cognitive control.**  
- Common among **corporate brainjackers, underground psychic thieves, and rogue mind-hackers.**  

#### **Archetype Abilities**  
| Level | Feature |  
|-------|---------|  
| 3rd | **Cognitive Tap** – Once per short rest, you can hear surface thoughts of a creature within 30 feet. |  
| 9th | **Memory Rewrite** – You can alter the memory of a creature you have physically touched in the last minute. They must make an Intelligence save or forget up to 1 minute. |  
| 13th | **Mind Veil** – You are immune to telepathic detection, mind reading, and any effect that would detect your thoughts. |  
| 17th | **Ego Wipe** – Once per long rest, you can force a target to make a Wisdom saving throw or have their identity temporarily erased for 1 minute. They forget their name, purpose, and allegiances. |  

---

### **The Circuitbreaker**  
*"I don’t bypass security—I crash the whole system."*  

#### **Features & Playstyle**  
- **Masters of technological disruption, sabotage, and hacking.**  
- Uses **EMP pulses, forced system shutdowns, and infrastructure manipulation.**  
- Common among **tech thieves, cyber-infiltrators, and rogue A.S.T.R.A.L. operatives.**  

#### **Archetype Abilities**  
| Level | Feature |  
|-------|---------|  
| 3rd | **Digital Saboteur** – Gain advantage on checks made to disable security systems, hack networks, or disrupt technology. |  
| 9th | **EMP Strike** – Once per short rest, you can make a melee attack that temporarily disables electronic devices and cybernetics within 10 feet. |  
| 13th | **System Erasure** – When you hack or disable a system, you can leave behind no digital trace of your presence. |  
| 17th | **Neural Shutdown** – Once per long rest, you can force a cybernetic or augmented enemy to make a Constitution save. On failure, they are completely disabled for 1 minute. |  

---

### **The Undertaker**  
*"Everyone ends up in my hands eventually."*  

#### **Features & Playstyle**  
- **Masters of body disposal, assassination, and escaping consequences.**  
- Uses **poisons, execution techniques, and corpse disposal skills.**  
- Common among **contract killers, death brokers, and crime syndicate enforcers.**  

#### **Archetype Abilities**  
| Level | Feature |  
|-------|---------|  
| 3rd | **Silent Kill** – If you reduce a creature to 0 HP with a melee attack, you can use a bonus action to make the body vanish for 1 hour. |  
| 9th | **Toxin Specialist** – Gain proficiency with poisoner’s kits. Your attacks can deliver poisons instantly without needing to coat weapons. |  
| 13th | **Death’s Shadow** – You are immune to being tracked by any means, including magical scrying, unless you choose to be found. |  
| 17th | **Clean Kill** – Once per long rest, if you kill a target, you can erase all evidence of their existence, including their name, records, and memory of them in nearby witnesses. |  

---

### **The Disruptor**  
*"A well-placed explosion fixes all problems."*  

#### **Features & Playstyle**  
- **Masters of urban demolition, high-impact sabotage, and environmental manipulation.**  
- Uses **explosives, improvised destruction, and structural collapse tactics.**  
- Common among **anarchists, mercenary saboteurs, and industrial wreckers.**  

\page

#### **Archetype Abilities**  
| Level | Feature |  
|-------|---------|  
| 3rd | **Demolition Expert** – Gain proficiency with explosives and knowledge of structural weaknesses. |  
| 9th | **Remote Detonation** – Once per short rest, you can place an explosive charge and detonate it at will within 300 feet. |  
| 13th | **Calculated Collapse** – You can rig a structure to collapse in a precise way, controlling the direction of its fall. |  
| 17th | **Chain Reaction** – Once per long rest, when an explosion occurs within 30 feet of you, you can cause a second explosion to occur as a free action. |  

---

### **The Silver Tongue**  
*"I don’t fight. I just make sure you fight for me."*  

#### **Features & Playstyle**  
- **Masters of deception, persuasion, and social engineering.**  
- Uses **manipulation, charm, and psychological warfare** instead of brute force.  
- Common among **con artists, corporate negotiators, and master deceivers.**  

#### **Archetype Abilities**  
| Level | Feature |  
|-------|---------|  
| 3rd | **Master of Lies** – Gain expertise in Persuasion and Deception. |  
| 9th | **Plant the Seed** – When you interact with a creature for at least 1 minute, you can subtly influence them into believing a lie for up to 24 hours. |  
| 13th | **Perfect Misdirection** – When an enemy targets you with an attack, you can use your reaction to force them to make a Wisdom save. On failure, they attack another target instead. |  
| 17th | **Master Manipulator** – Once per long rest, you can convince an NPC of anything for 1 hour, as long as it is not directly harmful to them. |  


## **Multiclassing**  
If your campaign allows multiclassing, use the following rules for a **Rogue** multiclass character.  

### **Ability Score Minimums**  
- Dexterity 13  

### **Proficiencies Gained**  
- Light armor, one skill of your choice, thieves’ tools  

---

## **Quick Build**  
You can make a **Rogue** quickly by following these suggestions:  
- Choose **Human or Gnome** for a thematic fit.  
- Pick the **Spy** or **Street Thief** background.  
- Prioritize **Dexterity**, followed by **Intelligence or Charisma**.  
- Take a silenced pistol and a hacking deck for maximum infiltration potential.
