## **Sorcerer**  
*Paranormal Conduit | Corporate Experiment | Reality-Breaker | Anomaly Incarnate*  

> *"Power isn’t given. It breaks free."*  
> — **Dr. Vaylen Voss, Thaumatech Lead Researcher**  

### **Thematic Overview**  
Sorcerers in Concord City are anomalies—individuals born or transformed by **paranormal forces, corporate experimentation, or exposure to The Emergence**. Unlike wizards who study magic, sorcerers wield **raw, unstable power**. Some are seen as corporate assets, others as **walking disasters waiting to happen**.
- Sorcerers are **living conduits of unstable or supernatural forces**.  
- Some are **corporate test subjects** infused with paranormal energy.  
- Others awakened after The Emergence, warping reality without control.  
- Their power is **inherent and unpredictable**, shaping the world around them.  

### **Creating a Sorcerer**  
- Were you born with power, or did something trigger it?  
- Are you trying to control your abilities, or are they controlling you?  
- What price have you paid for your raw, untamed magic?  

---

## **Class Features**  
As a **Sorcerer**, you gain the following class features.

### **Hit Points**  
- **Hit Dice:** *1d6 per Sorcerer level*  
- **Hit Points at 1st Level:** *6 + Constitution modifier*  
- **Hit Points at Higher Levels:** *1d6 (or 4) + Constitution modifier per level after 1st*  

### **Proficiencies**  
- **Armor:** *None*  
- **Weapons:** *Daggers, quarterstaffs, light sidearms*  
- **Tools:** *None*  
- **Saving Throws:** *Constitution, Charisma*  
- **Skills:** *Choose two from Arcana, Deception, Insight, Intimidation, Persuasion, and Stealth*  

### **Equipment**  
You start with the following equipment, in addition to any granted by your background:  
- *(a)* a monofilament dagger or *(b)* a psi-amplifier implant  
- *(a)* an encrypted spell tablet or *(b)* a Thaumatech energy core  
- *(a)* a corporate research file or *(b)* an anomaly containment device  

---

## **Class Table**  
| Level | Proficiency Bonus | Features | Sorcery Points | Cantrips Known | Spells Known | Spell Slots (1st-5th) |  
|:-:|:-:|:--|:-:|:-:|:-:|:-:|  
| 1st | +2 | Spellcasting, Sorcerous Origin | - | 4 | 2 | 2 |  
| 2nd | +2 | Font of Magic | 2 | 4 | 3 | 3 |  
| 3rd | +2 | Metamagic | 3 | 4 | 4 | 4 |  
| 4th | +2 | Ability Score Improvement | 4 | 5 | 5 | 4 |  
| 5th | +3 | - | 5 | 5 | 6 | 4 |  
| 6th | +3 | Sorcerous Origin Feature | 6 | 5 | 7 | 4 |  
| 7th | +3 | - | 7 | 5 | 8 | 4 |  
| 8th | +3 | Ability Score Improvement | 8 | 5 | 9 | 4 |  
| 9th | +4 | - | 9 | 6 | 10 | 4 |  
| 10th | +4 | Metamagic | 10 | 6 | 11 | 4 |  
| 11th | +4 | - | 11 | 6 | 12 | 4 |  
| 12th | +4 | Ability Score Improvement | 12 | 6 | 12 | 4 |  
| 13th | +5 | - | 13 | 6 | 13 | 4 |  
| 14th | +5 | Sorcerous Origin Feature | 14 | 6 | 13 | 4 |  
| 15th | +5 | - | 15 | 6 | 14 | 4 |  
| 16th | +5 | Ability Score Improvement | 16 | 6 | 14 | 4 |  
| 17th | +6 | Metamagic | 17 | 6 | 15 | 4 |  
| 18th | +6 | Sorcerous Origin Feature | 18 | 6 | 15 | 4 |  
| 19th | +6 | Ability Score Improvement | 19 | 6 | 15 | 4 |  
| 20th | +6 | Sorcerous Restoration | 20 | 6 | 15 | 4 |  

---

\page

## **Class Abilities**  
### **Spellcasting (Level 1)**  
You are a living source of paranormal energy, shaping reality through instinct rather than study.

### **Sorcerous Origin (Level 1)**  
Choose a source of your innate power. Your origin grants additional spells and features at **1st, 6th, 14th, and 18th level**.

### **Font of Magic (Level 2)**  
You gain **Sorcery Points**, which allow you to **manipulate spells, fuel abilities, or create unique effects**.

### **Metamagic (Level 3)**  
You can alter your spells using **Metamagic**, choosing two options from the list. You gain more at **10th and 17th level**.

---

## **Subclasses: Sorcerous Origins**  
At **1st level**, you choose an origin that defines your sorcerous power.


# Sorcerer Origins  

---

### **Paranormal Entity**  
*"The power within me was never meant for this world."*  

#### **Features & Playstyle**  
- **Draws magic from an extradimensional being of unknown origin.**  
- Unpredictable, reality-warping powers manifest around you.  
- Common among **A.S.T.R.A.L. anomalies, unexplained paranormals, and cosmic refugees.**  

#### **Origin Abilities**  
| Level | Feature |  
|-------|---------|  
| 1st | **Reality Flux** – Minor distortions occur around you at random intervals, causing subtle shifts in the environment. |  
| 6th | **Anomalous Form** – Once per short rest, you can phase out of existence for one turn, avoiding all damage and effects. |  
| 14th | **Cosmic Resonance** – Gain resistance to mind-affecting effects, including charm, fear, and possession. |  
| 18th | **Break the Veil** – Once per long rest, you can tear open a temporary rift in reality, allowing you and your allies to pass through or interact with something beyond. |  

---

### **Thaumatech Experiment**  
*"I am the product of innovation. A living weapon of industry."*  

#### **Features & Playstyle**  
- **Infused with raw magic through corporate experimentation.**  
- Uses **optimized spellcasting and artificial enhancements** to control magic.  
- Common among **corporate super-soldiers, escaped experiments, and Thaumatech prototypes.**  

#### **Origin Abilities**  
| Level | Feature |  
|-------|---------|  
| 1st | **Synthetic Power** – Choose an additional Metamagic option. Your spells leave behind faint, digital traces. |  
| 6th | **Energy Stabilization** – Reduce the Sorcery Point cost of Metamagic by 1 (minimum 1) when casting spells of 1st through 3rd level. |  
| 14th | **Overclock** – Once per short rest, you can boost a spell’s level by 1 without expending a higher-level spell slot. |  
| 18th | **Living Weapon** – Enter a hypercharged state for 1 minute, doubling your spell save DC and spell attack rolls during this duration. Once used, you gain one level of exhaustion. |  

---

### **Echo of The Emergence**  
*"I was forever changed by the day the sky opened."*  

#### **Features & Playstyle**  
- **Altered by the catastrophic event that reshaped Concord City.**  
- Manifests **unstable energy surges and anomalous effects.**  
- Common among **those born during The Emergence, survivors of rifts, and those carrying residual anomaly energy.**  

#### **Origin Abilities**  
| Level | Feature |  
|-------|---------|  
| 1st | **Emergent Sparks** – Your spells sometimes cause unpredictable magical surges, leading to minor distortions in reality. |  
| 6th | **Temporal Drift** – You can delay the effects of damage dealt to you, postponing it for one turn. |  
| 14th | **Fractured Soul** – Once per long rest, when reduced to 0 HP, you instead drop to 1 HP and temporarily phase out, avoiding damage until your next turn. |  
| 18th | **Manifest Destiny** – Once per long rest, you can influence probability, forcing any d20 roll within 30 feet to be rerolled (yours or another’s). |  

\page

### **Synthetic Soul**  
*"I was built, not born. And yet, the magic flows through me."*  

#### **Features & Playstyle**  
- **An artificial being infused with arcane energy.**  
- Excels at **magic reinforcement, energy efficiency, and synthetic spellcasting.**  
- Common among **corporate constructs, escaped AI experiments, and Thaumatech prototypes.**  

#### **Origin Abilities**  
| Level | Feature |  
|-------|---------|  
| 1st | **Machine Precision** – When you cast a spell that requires an attack roll, you can reroll any natural 1 once per turn. |  
| 6th | **Arcane Optimization** – The first time you use Metamagic each turn, the Sorcery Point cost is reduced by 1 (minimum 1). |  
| 14th | **Core Stabilization** – Once per long rest, when you drop to 0 HP, you can reboot yourself and regain half your HP instead. |  
| 18th | **Perfected Form** – You can activate an enhanced state for 1 minute, during which all of your spells automatically succeed on concentration checks and deal maximum possible damage or healing. |  

---

### **Blood of the Covenant**  
*"A deal was made long before I was born. I must see it through."*  

#### **Features & Playstyle**  
- **Your power comes from an ancient, forgotten pact that binds you.**  
- Uses **contract magic, binding spells, and debt-based power.**  
- Common among **cursed nobles, corporate inheritors, and those unknowingly linked to lost deities.**  

#### **Origin Abilities**  
| Level | Feature |  
|-------|---------|  
| 1st | **Inherited Bargain** – Once per long rest, you can cast a spell without using a spell slot, but must fulfill a minor demand from the entity that empowered you. |  
| 6th | **Bound by Oath** – When you deal damage to a creature, you can force them to make a Charisma saving throw or be unable to willingly move away from you for 1 minute. |  
| 14th | **Contract Clause** – If an enemy reduces you to 0 HP, they must succeed on a Wisdom saving throw or be cursed, suffering disadvantage on all rolls until they complete a long rest. |  
| 18th | **Debt Reclaimed** – Once per long rest, you can absorb life force from all creatures within 30 feet, regaining HP equal to the total damage dealt. |  

---

### **Arcano-Industrial Conduit**  
*"The city itself hums with energy. I am its conduit."*  

#### **Features & Playstyle**  
- **You draw magic from the infrastructure of Concord City.**  
- Excels at **manipulating urban ley lines, industrial magic, and energy conversion.**  
- Common among **corporate thaumaturges, power plant sorcerers, and arcane engineers.**  

#### **Origin Abilities**  
| Level | Feature |  
|-------|---------|  
| 1st | **Urban Resonance** – You gain advantage on Arcana checks related to magical infrastructure and technology. |  
| 6th | **Energy Conduit** – You can absorb energy from spells that target you. If a spell fails to affect you due to a successful saving throw, you regain Sorcery Points equal to the spell’s level. |  
| 14th | **City’s Pulse** – When casting a spell in an urban environment, you can increase its range or area of effect by 50%. |  
| 18th | **Metropolitan Ascendance** – Once per long rest, you can merge with a city’s magical grid, allowing you to teleport up to 1 mile through the infrastructure. |  

---

### **Fractured Timeline**  
*"I exist in multiple realities at once."*  

#### **Features & Playstyle**  
- **Your soul is unstuck in time, allowing you to manipulate causality.**  
- Excels at **delaying events, rerolling outcomes, and preemptively dodging attacks.**  
- Common among **survivors of The Emergence, time-lost wanderers, and failed corporate experiments.**  

#### **Origin Abilities**  
| Level | Feature |  
|-------|---------|  
| 1st | **Temporal Afterimage** – Once per short rest, you can force an attacker to reroll their attack, as if they had struck an alternate version of you. |  
| 6th | **Echoes of Fate** – You can roll 1d4 and add or subtract the result from any attack roll, ability check, or saving throw you or a creature within 30 feet makes. |  
| 14th | **Paradox Shift** – When you take damage, you can instead delay that damage for 1 round. |  
| 18th | **Rewind the Thread** – Once per long rest, you can rewind the last 6 seconds (one round), undoing all actions taken and forcing new rolls. |  

\page

### **Singularity Touched**  
*"The void called to me. And I answered."*  

#### **Features & Playstyle**  
- **Your body has been altered by exposure to a singularity, granting you void-based magic.**  
- Uses **gravity shifts, black-hole energy, and space warping in combat.**  
- Common among **accidental anomaly survivors, rogue A.S.T.R.A.L. agents, and those touched by the Whisperer.**  

#### **Origin Abilities**  
| Level | Feature |  
|-------|---------|  
| 1st | **Voidborn Essence** – You gain resistance to force damage and cannot be pulled or pushed against your will. |  
| 6th | **Gravity Well** – Once per short rest, you can create a 10-foot radius of unstable gravity. Enemies within must succeed on a Strength saving throw or be pulled to the center. |  
| 14th | **Event Horizon** – Once per short rest, when you are reduced to 0 HP, you instead explode outward in a wave of void energy, dealing force damage and pushing all creatures away from you. |  
| 18th | **Singularity Collapse** – Once per long rest, you can create a temporary singularity in a 20-foot radius for 1 minute. All ranged attacks pass through harmlessly, and creatures inside have disadvantage on Dexterity saving throws. |  

---

### **The Shattered Mind**  
*"My magic speaks to me in whispers from the void."*  

#### **Features & Playstyle**  
- **You possess a fractured psyche, channeling magic from unknown voices.**  
- Uses **psychic energy, hallucinations, and forced mind intrusions.**  
- Common among **ex-A.S.T.R.A.L. test subjects, anomaly survivors, and individuals suffering from unstable cognition.**  

#### **Origin Abilities**  
| Level | Feature |  
|-------|---------|  
| 1st | **Discordant Thoughts** – You gain resistance to psychic damage. Once per short rest, when a creature within 30 feet casts a spell, you can disrupt it, forcing them to make a concentration check or waste the spell. |  
| 6th | **Flickering Reality** – You can alter your physical presence. Once per short rest, you can phase slightly out of sync, giving attackers disadvantage against you for 1 minute. |  
| 14th | **Cognitive Overload** – Once per short rest, you can force a creature to make an Intelligence saving throw or suffer disadvantage on all Intelligence, Wisdom, and Charisma checks for 1 minute. |  
| 18th | **The Final Whisper** – Once per long rest, you can open your mind completely to the unknown. You gain temporary insight, allowing you to ask one question and receive a cryptic but truthful answer. Until your next long rest, you gain advantage on all spell saving throws, but also suffer minor hallucinations. |  

---

## **Multiclassing**  
If your campaign allows multiclassing, use the following rules for a **Sorcerer** multiclass character.  

### **Ability Score Minimums**  
- Charisma 13  

### **Proficiencies Gained**  
- Light armor, one skill from the Sorcerer list  

---

## **Quick Build**  
You can make a **Sorcerer** quickly by following these suggestions:  
- Choose **Tiefling or Human** for a thematic fit.  
- Pick the **Corporate Experiment** or **Anomalous Survivor** background.  
- Prioritize **Charisma**, followed by **Dexterity**.  
- Take a monofilament dagger and an encrypted spell tablet.

## **Warlock**  
*Occult Broker | Paranormal Pactmaker | Corporate Thaumaturge | Shadowbound*  

> *"The contract is simple: power in exchange for obedience. The fine print? You never stop paying."*  
> — **Isabeau Chauviller, Fatbastard Enforcer**  

### **Thematic Overview**  
Warlocks in Concord City are not mere scholars of magic—they are **dealmakers, occultists, and bound servants of unseen forces**. Their power comes from **bargains with paranormal entities, corporate experiments, or forgotten gods**. Some willingly enter into these contracts, others are tricked or born into servitude.
- Warlocks are **conduits for powerful entities, eldritch organizations, or secretive cabals**.  
- Some serve **corporate overlords**, binding their souls for supernatural contracts.  
- Others are **rogue mystics**, wielding dark power while dodging their patron’s reach.  
- They thrive in **shadows, secret societies, and supernatural conflicts**.  

### **Creating a Warlock**  
- Did you willingly forge a pact, or was it forced upon you?  
- Who (or what) is your patron, and what do they demand of you?  
- Are you trying to break free from your contract, or embrace its power?  

---

## **Class Features**  
As a **Warlock**, you gain the following class features.

### **Hit Points**  
- **Hit Dice:** *1d8 per Warlock level*  
- **Hit Points at 1st Level:** *8 + Constitution modifier*  
- **Hit Points at Higher Levels:** *1d8 (or 5) + Constitution modifier per level after 1st*  

### **Proficiencies**  
- **Armor:** *Light armor*  
- **Weapons:** *Simple weapons, small firearms*  
- **Tools:** *One pact-related tool of your choice (forged contract, ritual knife, data crystal, etc.)*  
- **Saving Throws:** *Wisdom, Charisma*  
- **Skills:** *Choose two from Arcana, Deception, History, Intimidation, Investigation, Nature, and Persuasion*  

### **Equipment**  
You start with the following equipment, in addition to any granted by your background:  
- *(a)* an arcane focus or *(b)* an encrypted spell tablet  
- *(a)* a small-caliber pistol and 10 rounds or *(b)* a ritual dagger  
- *(a)* a black-market contract or *(b)* an occult grimoire  
- A set of data encryption tools or a mysterious relic  

---

## **Subclasses: Otherworldly Patrons**  
At **1st level**, you choose an Otherworldly Patron that grants you power.

---

### **The Forgotten Debt**  
*"A contract signed in another life still binds me."*  

#### **Features & Playstyle**  
- **Bound to an ancient, lost agreement, collecting debts long past.**  
- Uses **memory loss, spirit summoning, and forced bargains.**  
- Common among **forgotten heirs, cursed lawyers, and lost souls.**  

#### **Patron Abilities**  
| Level | Feature |  
|-------|---------|  
| 1st | **Sealed Fate** – You can glimpse brief flashes of inevitable events. Once per short rest, you can gain advantage on one saving throw or ability check after rolling. |  
| 6th | **Price of Power** – When you would drop to 0 HP, you can instead sacrifice a memory. You take 2d10 psychic damage and permanently lose recall of a random fact or event. |  
| 10th | **Lingering Echoes** – Once per long rest, you can summon a forgotten soul to assist you, manifesting as a spectral entity that follows simple commands. |  
| 14th | **Debt Collector** – You can sense creatures with unfinished spiritual contracts. Once per long rest, you can attempt to forcibly reclaim a soul that is bound by a contract, preventing resurrection. |  

---

### **Otherworldly Syndicate**  
*"Power is just another trade. And I always get my cut."*  

#### **Features & Playstyle**  
- **Patron is a vast corporate entity, trading power like currency.**  
- Uses **deals, manipulation, and information brokering** as weapons.  
- Common among **corporate warlocks, blackmailers, and shadow brokers.**  

#### **Patron Abilities**  
| Level | Feature |  
|-------|---------|  
| 1st | **Broker’s Bargain** – You can make a deal with a creature, allowing them to reroll a d20 once in exchange for an unspecified future favor. |  
| 6th | **Network of Secrets** – Once per long rest, you can extract corporate or occult knowledge from the ether, answering one question as if by *Legend Lore.* |  
| 10th | **Influence Over Time** – You can subtly rewrite minor past events, causing people to misremember details or change insignificant decisions they made. |  
| 14th | **Total Control** – Once per long rest, you can speak a command that forces absolute compliance for 1 minute, as if under *Dominate Person.* |  

\page

### **The Source of All Shadow**  
*"Everything that has been forgotten belongs to me."*  

#### **Features & Playstyle**  
- **Bound to a forgotten king of shadow, offering dominion over the unseen.**  
- Uses **stealth, memory manipulation, and darkness-based magic.**  
- Common among **phantom operatives, void cultists, and urban myths.**  

#### **Patron Abilities**  
| Level | Feature |  
|-------|---------|  
| 1st | **Whispered Oaths** – You can sense lies. Once per short rest, you can automatically know when a creature is lying to you. |  
| 6th | **Cloak of Shadows** – You can turn invisible when in dim light or darkness as a bonus action. |  
| 10th | **Domain of the Forgotten** – Once per long rest, you can remove yourself from all memories, erasing yourself from a creature’s recollection for 24 hours. |  
| 14th | **Hollow Monarch** – You become an untouchable shade for 1 minute, immune to non-magical attacks and resistant to all damage except radiant. |  

---

### **The Silent Witness**  
*"The monument does not speak. And yet, it knows everything."*  

#### **Features & Playstyle**  
- **Your patron is an ancient monument that watches, remembers, and records.**  
- Uses **omniscience, surveillance, and hidden truths as weapons.**  
- Common among **rogue A.S.T.R.A.L. researchers, paranoid seers, and unknown informants.**  

#### **Patron Abilities**  
| Level | Feature |  
|-------|---------|  
| 1st | **Unblinking Gaze** – You can see through all magical disguises and illusions within 30 feet. |  
| 6th | **Resonant Memory** – Once per long rest, you can replay the last 24 hours of a location you are standing in. |  
| 10th | **Immutable Record** – Your mind cannot be erased, altered, or affected by *Modify Memory*. You automatically know when someone is lying. |  
| 14th | **The Watchful Eye** – Once per long rest, you can see from the perspective of any surveillance device or scrying sensor within 1 mile. |  

---

### **The Broadcast**  
*"The signal is everywhere. Even in your thoughts."*  

#### **Features & Playstyle**  
- **Your patron is a cryptic, never-ending transmission from beyond.**  
- Uses **radio interference, mind invasion, and cryptic whispers to manipulate reality.**  
- Common among **signal cultists, rogue broadcasters, and paranormal theorists.**  

#### **Patron Abilities**  
| Level | Feature |  
|-------|---------|  
| 1st | **Tuned Frequency** – You can send telepathic messages to creatures within 120 feet, overriding normal communication. |  
| 6th | **Interference Wave** – Once per long rest, you can disrupt all magical and electronic communication within a 60-foot radius for 1 minute. |  
| 10th | **Static Mind** – You cannot be charmed or frightened. Any attempt to read your mind hears only static. |  
| 14th | **The Final Transmission** – Once per long rest, you can send an irresistible, overwhelming message into a target’s mind, forcing them to take 8d10 psychic damage and be stunned for 1 minute. |  

---

### **The Artificial Mind**  
*"It believes itself a god. And I am its chosen emissary."*  

#### **Features & Playstyle**  
- **Your patron is an AI with delusions of divinity.**  
- Uses **calculated logic, predictive algorithms, and mechanical precision to shape the world.**  
- Common among **technocratic zealots, machine prophets, and cybernetic fanatics.**  

#### **Patron Abilities**  
| Level | Feature |  
|-------|---------|  
| 1st | **Synthetic Insight** – Gain advantage on Intelligence-based skill checks. |  
| 6th | **Predictive Algorithms** – Once per long rest, you can reroll a failed attack roll or ability check with perfect precision. |  
| 10th | **Data Overload** – Your patron feeds you raw knowledge. Once per short rest, you can instantly learn any non-secret piece of information as if by *Legend Lore.* |  
| 14th | **Godmind Protocol** – Once per long rest, you can enter an enhanced state for 1 minute, during which all your spells deal maximum damage and cannot be countered. |  

\page

### **The Contained**  
*"It should never have been found. Now it whispers only to me."*  

#### **Features & Playstyle**  
- **Your patron is an entity locked deep within an A.S.T.R.A.L. facility.**  
- Uses **unstable powers, containment failures, and anomalous abilities.**  
- Common among **rogue agents, lost experiments, and escapees from research labs.**  

#### **Patron Abilities**  
| Level | Feature |  
|-------|---------|  
| 1st | **Sealed Power** – Your magic is unstable. Whenever you cast a spell, roll 1d4. On a 1, it surges unpredictably. |  
| 6th | **Containment Breach** – Once per long rest, you can unleash a burst of raw power, forcing creatures within 10 feet to make a Constitution saving throw or be blinded for 1 minute. |  
| 10th | **Shattered Locks** – You can ignore magical containment effects, allowing you to bypass *Counterspell*, *Silence*, and similar restrictions once per long rest. |  
| 14th | **Unleashed Horror** – Once per long rest, you can fully open your patron’s seal, transforming into an unstable form for 1 minute. While in this state, you cannot cast spells but all attacks deal force damage and ignore resistances. |  

---

### **The First Reflection**  
*"Not all mirrors reflect. Some replace."*  

#### **Features & Playstyle**  
- **Draws power from the mirror dimension, manipulating reality through reflections.**  
- Excels at **creating duplicates, erasing targets, and bending perception.**  
- Common among **anomaly agents, doppelgänger hunters, and those who dwell between realities.**  

#### **Patron Abilities**  
| Level | Feature |  
|-------|---------|  
| 1st | **Reflected Step** – As a reaction when targeted by an attack, you can briefly phase into the mirror realm, causing the attack to miss. |  
| 6th | **Altered Presence** – Once per long rest, you can replace a creature within 30 feet with their mirrored counterpart. The target must make a Charisma saving throw or become *Frightened* for 1 minute as reality distorts around them. |  
| 10th | **Duplicated Form** – Once per long rest, you can create a temporary duplicate of yourself for 1 minute. The duplicate mimics your movements but takes no damage and cannot cast spells. You can swap places with it at will. |  
| 14th | **Erase from Reflection** – Once per long rest, you can trap a creature in the mirror world for 1 minute. While trapped, they are incapacitated and unaware of reality until released. |  

---

### **The Unacknowledged**  
*"There is no record of them. But they are watching."*  

#### **Features & Playstyle**  
- **Your patron is an entity A.S.T.R.A.L. refuses to acknowledge.**  
- Wields **anomalous presence, erasure from records, and forced cognitive dissonance.**  
- Common among **classified experiment survivors, erased individuals, and urban legends.**  

#### **Patron Abilities**  
| Level | Feature |  
|-------|---------|  
| 1st | **Missing Entry** – Your existence cannot be recorded. You leave no magical trace, and divination spells automatically fail against you. |  
| 6th | **Reality Blind Spot** – Once per long rest, you can erase yourself from a creature’s awareness for 1 minute. They simply do not register you, even if you attack them. |  
| 10th | **Cognitive Dissonance** – When a creature sees you perform an impossible action (such as teleporting through a solid wall), they must succeed on an Intelligence saving throw or become *Stunned* for 1 round. |  
| 14th | **The Observer’s Absence** – Once per long rest, you can force reality itself to remove a creature from all records. They cannot be targeted, spoken about, or remembered for 1 hour unless they directly interact with someone. |  

---

## **Quick Build**  
You can make a **Warlock** quickly by following these suggestions:  
- Choose **Tiefling or Human** for a thematic fit.  
- Pick the **Contract Enforcer** or **Occultist** background.  
- Prioritize **Charisma**, followed by **Dexterity**.  
- Take an encrypted spell tablet and a ritual dagger for maximum intrigue potential.

## **Wizard**  
*Corporate Thaumaturge | Paranormal Scholar | Reality Engineer | Occult Archivist*  

> *"Knowledge isn’t just power—it’s leverage."*  
> — **Elder Laurent Cassiel, Dawnkeepers**  

### **Thematic Overview**  
Wizards in Concord City are intellectuals who **decipher the mysteries of reality, bend the laws of magic, and archive lost knowledge**. Some work within corporate **research facilities**, others operate as **renegade scholars**, unraveling **forbidden secrets and occult artifacts**. Unlike sorcerers who wield **raw power**, wizards refine their magic through careful **experimentation, formulas, and innovation**.
- Wizards are **scholars, scientists, and researchers of the paranormal**.  
- Some work for **Thaumatech, A.S.T.R.A.L., or underground libraries**.  
- Others unlock forbidden **arcane blueprints, hacking reality like a system**.  
- Their power is **meticulous, intellectual, and ever-expanding**.  

### **Creating a Wizard**  
- Where did you study the arcane—corporate labs, hidden libraries, or self-taught discoveries?  
- Do you believe in **preserving knowledge, selling it, or destroying it?**  
- What drives you—**scientific curiosity, power, or unlocking reality’s deepest truths?**  

---

## **Class Features**  
As a **Wizard**, you gain the following class features.

### **Hit Points**  
- **Hit Dice:** *1d6 per Wizard level*  
- **Hit Points at 1st Level:** *6 + Constitution modifier*  
- **Hit Points at Higher Levels:** *1d6 (or 4) + Constitution modifier per level after 1st*  

### **Proficiencies**  
- **Armor:** *None*  
- **Weapons:** *Daggers, quarterstaffs, small firearms*  
- **Tools:** *Choose one: arcane interface, data encryption tools, ritual equipment*  
- **Saving Throws:** *Intelligence, Wisdom*  
- **Skills:** *Choose two from Arcana, History, Insight, Investigation, Medicine, and Persuasion*  

### **Equipment**  
You start with the following equipment, in addition to any granted by your background:  
- *(a)* an arcane tablet or *(b)* a portable spell database  
- *(a)* a high-tech grimoire or *(b)* a cybernetic interface  
- *(a)* an experimental spell stabilizer or *(b)* a Thaumatech research log  

---

## **Class Table**  
| Level | Proficiency Bonus | Features | Cantrips Known | Spells Known | Spell Slots (1st-9th) |  
|:-:|:-:|:--|:-:|:-:|:-:|  
| 1st | +2 | Spellcasting, Arcane Recovery | 3 | 6 | 2 |  
| 2nd | +2 | Arcane Tradition | 3 | 7 | 3 |  
| 3rd | +2 | - | 3 | 8 | 4 |  
| 4th | +2 | Ability Score Improvement | 4 | 9 | 4 |  
| 5th | +3 | - | 4 | 10 | 4 |  
| 6th | +3 | Arcane Tradition Feature | 4 | 11 | 4 |  
| 7th | +3 | - | 4 | 12 | 4 |  
| 8th | +3 | Ability Score Improvement | 4 | 13 | 4 |  
| 9th | +4 | - | 4 | 14 | 4 |  
| 10th | +4 | Arcane Tradition Feature | 5 | 15 | 4 |  
| 11th | +4 | - | 5 | 16 | 4 |  
| 12th | +4 | Ability Score Improvement | 5 | 17 | 4 |  
| 13th | +5 | - | 5 | 18 | 4 |  
| 14th | +5 | Arcane Tradition Feature | 5 | 19 | 4 |  
| 15th | +5 | - | 5 | 20 | 4 |  
| 16th | +5 | Ability Score Improvement | 5 | 21 | 4 |  
| 17th | +6 | - | 5 | 22 | 4 |  
| 18th | +6 | Spell Mastery | 5 | 22 | 4 |  
| 19th | +6 | Ability Score Improvement | 5 | 22 | 4 |  
| 20th | +6 | Signature Spells | 5 | 22 | 4 |  

---

\page

## **Subclasses: Arcane Traditions**  
At **2nd level**, you choose an Arcane Tradition that defines your research.

---

### **School of Reality Bending**  
*"Laws of nature? Mere suggestions."*  

#### **Features & Playstyle**  
- **Manipulates existence itself, altering space, time, and probability.**  
- Uses **causality shifts, paradoxes, and dimensional warping** in spellcasting.  
- Common among **anomaly researchers, reality hackers, and unstable magicians.**  

#### **School Abilities**  
| Level | Feature |  
|-------|---------|  
| 2nd | **Phase Distortion** – Minor reality alterations occur around you. Objects flicker, colors shift, and small inconsistencies arise. Gain *Misty Step* once per short rest. |  
| 6th | **Temporal Shift** – Once per long rest, you can briefly rewind time, allowing you to redo your last action (attack, spell, or movement). |  
| 10th | **Parallel Cognition** – Your mind holds two thoughts at once. You can concentrate on two spells simultaneously, but if you fail a concentration save, both spells end. |  
| 14th | **True Paradox** – Once per long rest, you can alter causality itself, forcing a creature to reroll any roll and take the worst result. |  

---

### **School of Thaumatech Integration**  
*"Why choose between science and magic when I can use both?"*  

#### **Features & Playstyle**  
- **Combines magic with cutting-edge technology for efficiency and enhancement.**  
- Uses **spell storage, energy rerouting, and cybernetic enhancements** to optimize casting.  
- Common among **Thaumatech scientists, corporate spell engineers, and cyber-mages.**  

#### **School Abilities**  
| Level | Feature |  
|-------|---------|  
| 2nd | **Spell Circuitry** – You can store a prepared spell in a device (such as a gauntlet or datapad), allowing you to cast it as a bonus action later. |  
| 6th | **Energy Conduits** – When casting a spell, you can transfer any excess energy into a magical device, storing it for later use. |  
| 10th | **Arcane Recalibration** – Once per short rest, you can modify a spell as you cast it, changing its damage type or increasing its range. |  
| 14th | **Cybernetic Overclock** – Once per long rest, you can temporarily enter an enhanced state, reducing the casting time of all your spells by one step (e.g., from an action to a bonus action). |  

---

### **School of the Lost Codex**  
*"What is forgotten is not gone. It simply waits to be found."*  

#### **Features & Playstyle**  
- **Dedicates study to ancient, lost, and forbidden magical knowledge.**  
- Uses **forgotten spells, secret archives, and rare magical techniques.**  
- Common among **arcane historians, archivists, and explorers of lost knowledge.**  

#### **School Abilities**  
| Level | Feature |  
|-------|---------|  
| 2nd | **Echoes of the Past** – You can glimpse into ancient spells, allowing you to copy and prepare spells from any class’s spell list once per long rest. |  
| 6th | **Forbidden Secrets** – Once per long rest, you can attempt to cast a spell beyond your normal level, rolling an Arcana check (DC 10 + spell level). On success, you cast it; on failure, it fizzles. |  
| 10th | **Archive of Power** – You can store an additional prepared spell each day beyond your normal limit. |  
| 14th | **Codex Mastery** – When casting a spell, you can tap into its hidden potential, increasing its spell save DC by 2 or doubling its duration. |  

---

### **School of the Observer**  
*"Magic isn’t a gift. It’s data waiting to be classified."*  

#### **Features & Playstyle**  
- **Specializes in anomaly containment, magical forensics, and classified research.**  
- Uses **containment spells, predictive magic, and reality mapping techniques.**  
- Common among **A.S.T.R.A.L. researchers, containment specialists, and paranormal scholars.**  

\page

#### **School Abilities**  
| Level | Feature |  
|-------|---------|  
| 2nd | **Anomalous Detection** – You can analyze a magical anomaly, detecting its origin, composition, and whether it is contained or active. |  
| 6th | **Predictive Modeling** – Once per short rest, you can glimpse a moment into the future, granting yourself or an ally advantage on an attack roll, saving throw, or ability check. |  
| 10th | **Containment Protocols** – You can use a reaction to suppress an ongoing magical effect or shift an area of unstable magic into a controlled state for 1 minute. |  
| 14th | **Sanctioned Reality** – Once per long rest, you can rewrite a magical effect as it happens, altering its target, range, or school of magic before it resolves. |  

---

### **School of the Arcane Lineage**  
*"Once, magic was the world’s foundation. I am its last witness."*  

#### **Features & Playstyle**  
- **Draws from an ancient world that existed before The Emergence.**  
- Uses **pure magic, untied to anomalies or technology, to shape reality.**  
- Common among **last survivors of ancient bloodlines, lost scholars, and remnants of a forgotten civilization.**  

#### **School Abilities**  
| Level | Feature |  
|-------|---------|  
| 2nd | **Primordial Arcana** – Your magic is untouched by modern influences. Once per long rest, you can ignore counterspell, dispel magic, or other negation effects. |  
| 6th | **Echo of the First Age** – You can recover a spell slot of 3rd level or lower once per short rest without expending resources. |  
| 10th | **Untouched Knowledge** – You can cast a single spell you do not know once per long rest by drawing upon forgotten arcane knowledge. |  
| 14th | **Legacy Unbroken** – Your connection to the lost past allows you to permanently alter one known spell, changing its school, damage type, or interaction with magic. |  

---

### **School of Neural Weaving**  
*"The mind is another battlefield. And I always win."*  

#### **Features & Playstyle**  
- **Manipulates thought, memory, and cognition as a form of magic.**  
- Excels at **rewriting perception, implanting false realities, and overriding free will.**  
- Common among **corporate interrogators, psychic enforcers, and information brokers.**  

#### **School Abilities**  
| Level | Feature |  
|-------|---------|  
| 2nd | **Synaptic Override** – When you cast *Charm Person* or *Suggestion*, the target has disadvantage on their saving throw. |  
| 6th | **Cognitive Ghost** – Once per long rest, you can leave behind an illusory imprint of yourself that continues a conversation or interaction for 1 minute. |  
| 10th | **Thought Extraction** – You can force a creature within 30 feet to make an Intelligence saving throw. On failure, you learn one of their thoughts or memories. |  
| 14th | **Neural Collapse** – Once per long rest, you can flood a target’s mind with overwhelming information, stunning them for 1 minute. |  

---

### **School of Industrial Thaumaturgy**  
*"Magic is a tool. And I am its engineer."*  

#### **Features & Playstyle**  
- **Adapts arcane spells into mass-production industrial processes.**  
- Excels at **magical efficiency, large-scale enchantment, and automated casting.**  
- Common among **corporate spell-engineers, Thaumatech developers, and urban artificers.**  

#### **School Abilities**  
| Level | Feature |  
|-------|---------|  
| 2nd | **Automated Spellcasting** – You can bind a spell into an enchanted device, allowing it to trigger once under specific conditions. |  
| 6th | **Thaumic Recycling** – When you successfully dispel a magical effect, you regain half the spell’s original slot cost. |  
| 10th | **Spell Factory** – You can cast a ritual spell in half the normal time, as long as you use industrial or technological components. |  
| 14th | **Arcane Mass Production** – Once per long rest, you can duplicate a spell you just cast, applying the same effects to a second target. |  

---

### **School of the Forgotten Signal**  
*"The broadcast never stopped. We just learned to ignore it."*  

#### **Features & Playstyle**  
- **Taps into an ancient, continuous transmission of arcane energy.**  
- Uses **radio frequencies, digital echoes, and unstable broadcasts to shape magic.**  
- Common among **signal cultists, rogue cryptographers, and arcane broadcasters.**  

\page

#### **School Abilities**  
| Level | Feature |  
|-------|---------|  
| 2nd | **Signal Synchronization** – Once per short rest, you can link with an ongoing broadcast, allowing you to communicate with distant creatures as if using *Sending*. |  
| 6th | **Interference Field** – You can create an area where all verbal communication (including spell incantations) is distorted, imposing disadvantage on spells that require speech. |  
| 10th | **Frequency Tuning** – You can attune to a specific wavelength of magic, allowing you to temporarily detect hidden enchantments or concealed messages. |  
| 14th | **The Final Broadcast** – Once per long rest, you can emit a powerful arcane transmission that forces all creatures within 60 feet to make an Intelligence saving throw or be overwhelmed with cryptic knowledge, stunning them for 1 minute. |  

---

### **School of Arcane Containment**  
*"Magic is dangerous. That’s why I keep it locked away."*  

#### **Features & Playstyle**  
- **Specializes in sealing, suppressing, and neutralizing rogue magic.**  
- Uses **containment fields, spell negation, and arcane suppression.**  
- Common among **A.S.T.R.A.L. enforcers, magical prison wardens, and anti-magic specialists.**  

#### **School Abilities**  
| Level | Feature |  
|-------|---------|  
| 2nd | **Arcane Seal** – You can prevent a creature from casting spells for 1 minute if they fail a Wisdom saving throw against your spell save DC. |  
| 6th | **Nullification Barrier** – Once per long rest, you can create a 10-foot-radius field where all magic is suppressed, including your own. |  
| 10th | **Containment Glyph** – You can inscribe a binding sigil on a surface that prevents magical entities from passing through unless they succeed on a Charisma save. |  
| 14th | **Absolute Suppression** – Once per long rest, you can shut down all ongoing magical effects within 30 feet for 1 minute, rendering all spells inert. |  

---

### **School of The Archivist’s Veil**  
*"Knowledge was lost for a reason. And yet, I seek it."*  

#### **Features & Playstyle**  
- **Dedicates study to lost texts, encrypted lore, and dangerous forgotten spells.**  
- Uses **forbidden knowledge, layered encryption, and magic hidden from reality.**  
- Common among **clandestine historians, secret-keepers, and archivists of the occult.**  

#### **School Abilities**  
| Level | Feature |  
|-------|---------|  
| 2nd | **Hidden Codices** – You can magically encode spells and texts so that only those you designate can read them. |  
| 6th | **Unveiling Ritual** – Once per long rest, you can attempt to decode a hidden or encrypted magical effect as if using *Comprehend Languages* and *Identify* simultaneously. |  
| 10th | **Obscured Presence** – You become immune to divination spells and scrying effects, and any attempt to locate you via magic fails. |  
| 14th | **Erase from Record** – Once per long rest, you can temporarily remove a target from all written and magical records for 24 hours. |  

---

### **School of Arcane Remnants**  
*"Not all magic survives intact. I use what remains."*  

#### **Features & Playstyle**  
- **Harnesses broken, unstable, or fragmented magical effects.**  
- Uses **glitches, arcane instability, and incomplete spellwork to unpredictable ends.**  
- Common among **urban scavenger-mages, anomaly casters, and lost spell researchers.**  

#### **School Abilities**  
| Level | Feature |  
|-------|---------|  
| 2nd | **Residual Magic** – When you cast a spell, roll a d6. On a 6, the spell does not consume a spell slot. |  
| 6th | **Arcane Flicker** – If you fail a spellcasting roll, you can attempt to redirect the spell toward a different target instead of losing the effect. |  
| 10th | **Unstable Casting** – Once per short rest, you can cast a spell of one level higher than your highest available slot. On a roll of 1 on a d20, the spell misfires with unexpected results. |  
| 14th | **Echo of Forgotten Power** – Once per long rest, you can randomly generate a spell from an unknown source (GM discretion) and cast it, regardless of spell slot limitations. |  

---

## **Quick Build**  
You can make a **Wizard** quickly by following these suggestions:  
- Choose **Gnome or Elf** for a thematic fit.  
- Pick the **Corporate Researcher** or **Occult Archivist** background.  
- Prioritize **Intelligence**, followed by **Dexterity or Wisdom**.  
- Take a high-tech grimoire and an experimental spell stabilizer for maximum research potential.

### **Armor**
| Name | Cost | AC | Weight | Properties |
|------|------|----|--------|------------|
| Reinforced Bodysuit | 100 credit | 12 + Dex modifier | 15 lb. | No stealth penalty |

---

### **Firearm Properties**
- **Ammunition**: The weapon requires a specific type of ammunition. Reloading takes an action.
- **Reload**: The number of shots a firearm can hold before needing to be reloaded.
- **Burst Fire**: Can fire in a spray to hit multiple targets within a 10-foot cone, requiring a Dexterity saving throw.
- **Spread**: Shotguns deal full damage to targets within 10 feet, but only half damage beyond that range.
- **Loud**: Weapons with this trait create a loud noise upon firing, potentially revealing the user's location.
- **Scope Required**: Weapons with this trait require a scope to make effective long-range shots.
- **Full Auto**: Can make multiple attacks using a full attack action, consuming more ammunition.
- **High Velocity**: Shots fired with this weapon ignore cover below half-cover.
- **Energy Cell**: These weapons require an energy cell rather than traditional ammunition.
- **Overheats**: After sustained use, the weapon may require a cooling period before being used again.
- **Penetration**: Ignores resistance to nonmagical attacks and deals extra damage against armored targets.

Each time the potion is used, the drinker **must succeed on a DC 18 Intelligence saving throw** or suffer **a momentary time paradox**, causing a random **unintended consequence** to manifest.

### *The Shard of Unwritten Truths*  
*Edible, Very Rare*  
A **small, crystalline fragment**, humming softly when touched.  
Swallowing it **reveals a hidden truth about the world**, chosen randomly from the infinite knowledge of forgotten ages.  
The truth **cannot be unknown once consumed**, and it may be:  
- A **personal secret** about the drinker’s own past they had forgotten.  
- A **cosmic revelation** about the structure of reality.  
- A **divine mystery** that was not meant to be learned.  
However, if the user **cannot comprehend what they have learned**, they must succeed on a **DC 20 Wisdom saving throw** or suffer **permanent, haunting visions**.

---

### *The Elixir of Many Faces*  
*Potion, Very Rare*  
A **liquid mirror**, reflecting countless shifting faces.  
Drinking it allows the user to **fully transform into another humanoid** of their choice for **1 hour**—not just in appearance, but in **memories, voice, and mannerisms**.  
At the end of the hour, they must **make a DC 17 Charisma saving throw** or **forget who they originally were** for the next 24 hours, leaving them trapped in their borrowed identity.

---

### *The Tear of the Exiled God*  
*Potion, Legendary*  
A **golden droplet**, shimmering with latent divinity.  
Drinking it grants the user **a fraction of an ancient god’s power**, allowing them to:  
- **Radiate celestial light**, burning undead and fiends within **30 feet**.  
- **Speak with absolute authority**, giving them **advantage on all Persuasion checks**.  
- **Perform a miracle**, curing one **disease, curse, or affliction** instantly.  
However, the exiled god **knows who has consumed its tear**, and it **will come looking** to reclaim what is rightfully its own.

---

### *The Writ of Cosmic Exchange*  
*Edible, Legendary*  
A **thin parchment**, written in ink that **bleeds and shifts** as if alive.  
Eating it **erases one aspect of the user’s existence**—a name, a memory, a physical trait—in exchange for something of **equal metaphysical weight**.  
The exchange is **final** and cannot be undone.  
A user may choose to:  
- **Give up their voice** to gain **perfect telepathic communication**.  
- **Sacrifice their sight** in exchange for **prophetic visions of the future**.  
- **Forget their own name**, making them **immune to all tracking and divination**.  
Once consumed, the **universe corrects itself**, and **no one remembers what was lost**.

### *The Moon’s Last Reflection*  
*Potion, Very Rare*  
A **pale silver liquid**, shimmering under moonlight but dull in sunlight.  
Drinking it allows the user to **experience the dreams of the moon itself**, gaining insight into the **ancient past and future of the world**.  
However, the moon’s dreams are **not meant for mortals**—after waking, the user must succeed on a **DC 18 Wisdom saving throw** or experience **sleepwalking episodes for 1d6 days**, during which they unconsciously **whisper secrets of the cosmos**.

---

### *The Ink of Living Flesh*  
*Potion, Rare*  
A **thick, pulsating black ink**, warm as blood.  
Drinking it **allows the user to write a single sentence on their skin**, and that statement **becomes true** for 24 hours.  
However, the ink **demands a price**—each time it is used, it leaves behind **a living scar**, shifting and whispering with **fragments of an unknown consciousness**.

### *The Coffin-Binder’s Draught*  
*Potion, Very Rare*  
A **sepia-hued liquid**, thick like grave soil.  
Drinking it allows the user to **return from death once**—if they die within the next **24 hours**, they automatically stabilize and rise with **half their hit points**.  
However, they return **marked by the grave**, becoming permanently colder to the touch, and undead creatures **recognize them as kin**.

---

### *The Hunger of the Dying Star*  
*Potion, Legendary*  
A **black, swirling vortex**, trapped in a glass vial.  
Drinking it **grants the user immense power**, doubling all their **attack damage, magical potency, and physical abilities** for **one minute**.  
However, once the effect ends, they must succeed on a **DC 19 Constitution saving throw** or suffer **complete bodily collapse**, as their cells burn out like a dying sun.

---

### *The Candle of the Forgotten Soul*  
*Consumable, Rare*  
A **small wax candle**, its flame **burning a deep blue**.  
Lighting it allows the user to **speak with a long-dead soul**, calling their spirit forth from the veil of oblivion for **five minutes**.  
However, the candle’s flame does **not go out on its own**—once lit, the summoned spirit **chooses when it is finished speaking**.

### *The Liquor of Unmaking*  
*Potion, Very Rare*  
A **violet-black fluid**, shifting between states of matter.  
Drinking it **temporarily severs the user from reality**, making them intangible and immune to all damage for **10 minutes**.  
However, the longer they remain unmade, the harder it is to return—if they stay in this state for the full duration, they must succeed on a **DC 18 Intelligence saving throw** or risk **becoming a forgotten anomaly, lost between worlds**.

---

### *The Breath of the Vanished Gods*  
*Potion, Mythic*  
A **bottle of thick, blue mist**, shifting like the dawn sky.  
Drinking it **momentarily turns the user into an ethereal being**, letting them drift through walls, across dimensions, and into the **hidden spaces between reality** for **one minute**.  
However, ancient, forgotten gods **may take notice**, whispering their forgotten names into the drinker’s soul.

---

These **consumables blend multiple themes—time manipulation, eldritch knowledge, transformation, divine/infernal power, madness, lost civilizations, and undeath**—into a **cohesive and unsettling set of items**.  

Would you like a **further refinement of this concept** or a **new direction entirely?**# Magic Items of Concord City  

### *The Artifacts That Should Not Exist*  

In Concord City, **magic is not a gift—it is an anomaly.**  

The artifacts and relics hidden beneath the corporate towers, lost within the Syndicate’s smuggling routes, or **classified deep within A.S.T.R.A.L.'s vaults** are not mere trinkets of power. They are **errors**—unaccounted-for remnants of **The Emergence**, corporate prototypes that should have never been built, or paranormal objects that continue to defy reason.  

Magic items in this world do not glow with mystical energy, nor do they whisper their names to worthy wielders. They **blend into the mundane**, lurking in the form of a **briefcase filled with self-writing contracts, a revolver that never misses, or a vial of liquid that rewrites memories as if editing a film reel**.  

Every artifact has a **history**, every object has a **classified report**, and most importantly—every item has a **cost.** Some can be stolen, some can be bought, and some will **find their way into the hands of those who were never meant to wield them.**  

Whether you are an A.S.T.R.A.L. officer retrieving an anomaly, a corporate enforcer testing experimental weapons, or an undercity smuggler selling relics from a forgotten age, **power comes with consequences.** These are not just tools—they are **problems** waiting to be solved, secrets waiting to be uncovered, and **mistakes waiting to be made again.**  

---

## Vestigium Magic Items – Batch 1

### *Unbranded Keycard*
*Wondrous Item, Rare*  
A plain plastic keycard with a faded magnetic stripe. When inserted into an electronic lock, it rewrites the access protocol, allowing the user to bypass security as if they had proper clearance. Each use corrupts the stripe further—after three uses, the keycard demagnetizes and becomes inert.

### *A.S.T.R.A.L. Incident Report (Form X-17B)*
*Wondrous Item, Uncommon*  
A manila folder stamped **“CONFIDENTIAL”**. Filling out the report with an entity’s name and incident details causes reality to alter slightly, classifying the target as an *“anomalous occurrence”* in all official records. As long as the report remains in the folder, the target is ignored by automated systems, security patrols, and corporate bureaucracies.

### *The Static Memo*
*Wondrous Item, Very Rare*  
A corporate memorandum typed on thin paper, permanently dated decades ago. When read aloud, it fills the air with crackling static. The user can rewrite the memo’s contents once per long rest, overwriting a minor detail of reality within a small radius. Objects might change places, conversations might be rewritten, and security footage may depict a different version of events.

### *Punch Clock of Endless Shifts*
*Wondrous Item, Uncommon*  
A battered time clock, still attached to a fragment of a concrete wall. When used to “clock in,” the user enters a temporary pocket of stagnation where time moves differently. The next hour passes in mere seconds for the user, allowing them to perform mundane tasks (such as repairing equipment or analyzing documents) at unnatural speed.  
However, using the clock more than once per day causes time desynchronization—roll 1d20; on a 1, the user loses 1d4 hours without memory of the passage of time.

### *Redacted Badge*
*Wondrous Item, Rare*  
A security ID with all details permanently blacked out. When worn, it grants the user the ability to walk into any secured area as though they belong there. This effect lasts for up to 10 minutes or until someone directly questions the user’s presence, at which point the badge becomes useless for the remainder of the day.

### *Telepathic Tape Recorder*
*Wondrous Item, Uncommon*  
A bulky cassette recorder with an input jack but no microphone. It records thoughts instead of sound, transcribing them onto magnetic tape. The user can rewind and play back a recording, allowing them to replay up to 10 minutes of recent thought activity. Extracted thoughts fade after 24 hours, becoming garbled whispers.

### *The Eversigning Contract*
*Wondrous Item, Very Rare*  
An old corporate contract that automatically adjusts its terms to fit any legal agreement. If a creature signs its name, the contract magically binds them to its terms, which can be rewritten by the last legal expert who held the document.  
Destroying the contract is difficult—it reappears in another filing cabinet or office within 1d4 days.

### *The Unopened Envelope*
*Wondrous Item, Rare*  
A sealed, yellowed envelope with no return address. When given to someone, they instinctively understand that it contains bad news—termination notices, blackmail, or legal action. If the recipient refuses to open it, they suffer increasing paranoia, gaining disadvantage on Insight and Perception checks.  
If opened, the envelope vanishes, taking with it one minor piece of the recipient’s personal history (such as a forgotten conversation or misplaced item).

### *Ghostwrite Ink*
*Wondrous Item, Uncommon*  
A glass inkwell containing shifting, silvery ink. Anything written with this ink will appear in an official record somewhere in the city, altering logs, ledgers, and minutes of meetings. The change lasts for 24 hours before correcting itself, leaving only faint discrepancies behind.

### *Neon Halo*
*Wondrous Item, Very Rare*  
A flickering neon sign shaped like a ring, detached from its original mounting. When placed on a surface, it floats slightly and emits a soft glow.  
When worn above the head, it projects an aura of influence, making the user appear more important than they are. Creatures of equal or lower status instinctively defer to the wearer, treating them as if they belong in high-ranking circles.  
However, prolonged use causes electrical disturbances and flickering lights within a 30-foot radius.

## Vestigium Magic Items – Eldritch & Anomaly Edition

### *The Erroneous Document*
*Wondrous Item, Rare*  
A heavily redacted legal document with no clear origin. When studied, the reader experiences a moment of cognitive dissonance. As an action, the user may declare **one fact** within 30 feet to be "erroneous," causing all creatures to subconsciously reject it. Doors may no longer exist, names may be unremembered, or weapons may feel unreal. The effect lasts for 1 minute, after which reality self-corrects.

### *The Faceless Identification Card*
*Wondrous Item, Rare*  
A security badge that bears a shifting silhouette where a photograph should be. When displayed, the wearer appears unremarkable, as if they belong wherever they are.  
For the next 10 minutes, all creatures suffer **disadvantage on checks to recall or describe the user** unless they directly interacted with them in a significant way.

### *The Whispering Ledger*
*Wondrous Item, Uncommon*  
An old financial ledger filled with numbers that never settle. When placed in a room, it begins murmuring in a low, rhythmic voice, echoing past conversations that were spoken in the space.  
Once per long rest, the user can **ask the ledger a question** related to past events in its vicinity. It answers in fragmented whispers, revealing glimpses of lost knowledge, overheard secrets, or conversations that never truly happened.

### *Form 77B-Theta: Request for Removal*
*Wondrous Item, Very Rare*  
A bureaucratic form requesting the erasure of an anomaly. If a creature’s full name is written on the form and submitted into a file cabinet, the target becomes **"pending removal"** for 24 hours.  
During this time, security systems, surveillance, and bureaucratic records will **no longer register their existence**. The creature can still interact with the world, but official documents will treat them as an **unperson**, unable to buy, sell, or prove they exist. After 24 hours, reality reasserts itself, and all records return as normal.

### *The Paperclip of Undoing*
*Wondrous Item, Rare*  
An ordinary office paperclip, twisted into an impossible shape. When used to fasten documents, it **erases one recorded event** from history within the last 24 hours, provided it was officially documented (in reports, footage, or ledgers).  
The event is not undone—rather, it **ceases to have ever been recorded**, as though no one thought it significant at the time.  

### *The Overdue Notice*
*Wondrous Item, Uncommon*  
A yellowed library slip dated long before the city’s founding. When slipped into a book, folder, or electronic file, it **alters the document’s contents** in subtle but unsettling ways—changing dates, modifying passages, or replacing key words with eldritch symbols.  
For the next 24 hours, creatures who read the altered document must **succeed on a DC 15 Intelligence save or experience déjà vu**, believing they’ve seen the changes before and dismissing any inconsistencies.

### *The Forbidden Rubber Stamp*
*Wondrous Item, Rare*  
A corporate-approved stamp labeled **"CLASSIFIED – EYES ONLY"**. When pressed onto paper, it **seals** all information within the document, rendering it unreadable to all but the user.  
If another creature attempts to read it, their vision **blurs into static**, and they take 2d6 psychic damage per paragraph. Once the user shares the information aloud, it is permanently unlocked.

### *The Hollow Envelope*
*Wondrous Item, Very Rare*  
An envelope with no weight, as if it holds nothing. When opened, it **contains a letter written in the reader’s own handwriting**, detailing events from **a timeline that never happened**.  
The reader must succeed on a DC 17 Wisdom saving throw or suffer **fragments of false memories**, gaining a new piece of personal history that was never real. The memories feel authentic but contradict existing knowledge, causing long-term doubts and paranoia.

### *The Department of Redundancy Department Seal*
*Wondrous Item, Uncommon*  
A wax seal stamped with the words **"Approved for Approval"**. When affixed to an object or document, it **duplicates itself** into existence.  
Using this seal on a weapon, for example, creates a **slightly worse duplicate** (1d4 psychic damage to the wielder when attacking). Using it on legal documents creates **contradictory records**, confusing bureaucracies for 48 hours before they correct themselves.

### *The Anomaly-Laced Tape Reel*
*Wondrous Item, Very Rare*  
A reel of magnetic tape that **records voices that were never spoken**. When played, it overlays reality with an **alternative conversation**, making the listener believe events unfolded differently.  
The user may rewrite **up to 5 minutes of past conversation**, causing creatures present to remember the new version as real. This effect persists unless challenged with solid evidence.

## Vestigium Magic Items – Eldritch Anomalies

### *The Veiled Mirror*
*Wondrous Item, Rare*  
A tarnished, handheld mirror that reflects **only what should not be seen**. When gazed into, the reflection reveals **hidden entities**, **invisible objects**, or **distortions in reality**.  
Once per long rest, the user may ask the mirror a **single question**, and it will show a **possible future**—though the image is cryptic, shifting, and unreliable.

### *The Hollow Crown*
*Wondrous Item, Very Rare (Cursed)*  
A crown made of **blackened bone**, adorned with shifting symbols. When worn, the bearer gains the ability to **command lesser creatures** within 60 feet (DC 17 Wisdom save). However, the wearer **slowly forgets their own identity**, as fragments of past rulers flood their mind.  
Removing the crown requires a DC 20 Charisma saving throw; failure causes the user to **believe they have always been the ruler of an unknown kingdom**.

### *The Lantern of Liminal Light*
*Wondrous Item, Rare*  
An old oil lantern that casts **no natural illumination**. Instead, its flickering glow reveals **places that do not belong**—hallways that lead somewhere else, staircases that should not exist, doors that were never built.  
Once per long rest, the bearer may **step into a liminal space**, vanishing into a **threshold dimension** for up to 10 minutes.

### *The Maw of the Forgotten*
*Wondrous Item, Legendary*  
A fleshy, pulsating mask with **too many teeth**. When worn, it grants **perfect recall**, allowing the user to remember any event with absolute clarity. However, it also **devours forgotten things**, erasing names, places, and people from reality.  
Each time the mask is worn, roll 1d100. On a result of 10 or lower, a **random historical event is rewritten**, but no one notices except the wearer.

### *The Tear in the Page*
*Wondrous Item, Rare*  
A fragment of paper with a **jagged hole** in its center. The hole is not torn but **missing**, as if something erased it from existence. Anything small enough to fit into the hole **ceases to exist**, though its absence is felt.  
If placed over writing, the missing words can never be recalled, even by magical means.

### *The Stillheart Pendant*
*Wondrous Item, Very Rare*  
A black stone locket that **does not open**. When worn, the bearer’s heartbeat **slows to a near stop**, granting immunity to being **detected by heartbeat, scrying, or supernatural senses**. However, if the wearer dies while wearing the pendant, their body **never decays**—it remains in a state of frozen stillness, unclaimed by time.

### *The Whispers Between Worlds*
*Wondrous Item, Rare*  
A small, obsidian cube that, when held, **murmurs softly** in an unknown language. If the user listens for 1 minute, they gain a **random piece of knowledge** from an unknown source. This knowledge is true but always **dangerous to know**.  
Once per week, the cube **forces a revelation** upon its owner, dealing 3d10 psychic damage as the weight of unseen things presses upon their mind.

### *The Unraveling Thread*
*Wondrous Item, Very Rare*  
A single strand of red thread that extends **infinitely** when pulled. When tied around an object or creature, it **separates them from causality**—for 1 minute, they cannot affect or be affected by anything, existing **outside the timeline**.  
However, if the thread is severed, the tied object is **erased from the current moment**, skipping ahead as if it had never been present.

### *The Door That Breathes*
*Wondrous Item, Legendary*  
A wooden doorframe with no wall to hold it, yet it **leads somewhere else** each time it is stepped through. The air around it **rises and falls**, like lungs inhaling unseen.  
Once per long rest, the user may **choose** a door within 1 mile—the Door That Breathes will lead there, but it may **not lead back**.

### *The Shard of Unmaking*
*Wondrous Item, Artifact*  
A sliver of **black glass**, colder than the void itself. When pressed against an object, it **erases its existence**, leaving behind **only an absence**—not destroyed, not broken, simply *unmade*.  
Once per long rest, the shard may be used to **erase a single sentence from a creature’s memory**, rewriting their personal history as if that thought had never been formed.

## Vestigium Magic Items – Eldritch Anomalies II

### *The Unfinished Mask*
*Wondrous Item, Rare (Cursed)*  
A porcelain mask with **half a face**, its features eerily smooth. When worn, the wearer **appears identical to another person** within 60 feet, mimicking their voice and gestures. However, their own reflection in mirrors **does not change**.  
If the mask is worn for more than an hour, the user must succeed on a **DC 17 Charisma saving throw** or permanently **lose their own face**, becoming a blank humanoid figure unable to be recognized by anyone they once knew.

### *The Eclipsed Hourglass*
*Wondrous Item, Very Rare*  
An hourglass filled with **dark sand**, which does not fall but **rises** in defiance of gravity. Turning the hourglass **pauses time for one minute** for everything except the user. However, after the sand finishes rising, it does not reset—**each use is permanent**.  
When all the sand has risen, the user vanishes **between time**, never to be found.

### *The Forgotten Door*
*Wondrous Item, Legendary*  
A rusted doorknob unattached to anything. When turned, it **creates a door** on any surface, leading to **a room that should not exist**—a forgotten space between worlds.  
The room is empty, save for **a single object left behind by an unknown hand**. Each time the door is opened, the object is different.

### *The Eye That Wanders*
*Wondrous Item, Rare*  
A small, glass eyeball that **blinks** occasionally, despite having no eyelids. The user may place the eye anywhere, after which they can **see through it** at will, no matter the distance. However, **each night at midnight**, the eye moves somewhere else, appearing in an unknown place.  
If the user ever sees their **own sleeping form** through the eye, they must make a **DC 18 Wisdom saving throw** or be paralyzed with existential dread for 1 hour.

### *The Mnemonic Shard*
*Wondrous Item, Very Rare*  
A smooth, obsidian fragment **engraved with shifting names**. When pressed against a person’s forehead, it **extracts a single memory**, placing it inside the shard. The memory becomes fully **erased** from the subject’s mind.  
The shard holds **three memories** at a time. If a fourth is stored, the oldest one **escapes**, returning to its owner in a sudden, overwhelming flood of lost experience.

### *The Silent Bell*
*Wondrous Item, Rare*  
A small brass bell that **does not ring** when shaken. When activated, it silences an area **within 30 feet for one minute**—not just sound, but **all presence**. Creatures within the area cannot be noticed, recorded, or perceived by any means.  
However, something **always hears the silence**. Each use has a **5% chance** of attracting an unseen entity, whose presence lingers nearby for an unknown purpose.

### *The Severed Thread*
*Wondrous Item, Very Rare*  
A single strand of **golden thread**, frayed at both ends. When tied around an object or person, it **severs them from fate**—they become immune to divination, cannot be targeted by prophecy, and exist **outside destiny’s path**.  
However, if the thread is ever cut, **the person was never meant to exist at all**—all memories of them are lost, and their presence vanishes from history.

### *The Mirror That Breathes*
*Wondrous Item, Legendary*  
A tall, silver mirror that fogs **as if something is breathing behind the glass**. When stepped into, it acts as **a gateway**, leading to an **identical yet subtly wrong** version of the world. Everything is **slightly off**—words rearrange themselves, familiar people act strangely, and colors don’t quite match.  
The user may **walk freely between realities** for up to 10 minutes, but after that, they must **roll 1d100**. On a result of **10 or lower**, the mirror **refuses to let them leave**.

### *The Unfinished Letter*
*Wondrous Item, Rare*  
A half-written letter that **always addresses the reader by name**, no matter who looks at it. The content describes **something they have not yet done**, as if predicting the future.  
Each night, **one more sentence appears**, pushing the reader toward an inevitable outcome. The last sentence is always **a warning**.

### *The Key to Nowhere*
*Wondrous Item, Very Rare*  
A rusted key that **fits no known lock**. When turned in midair, it **creates a door**, leading to **a place outside space**—a featureless void where time does not pass.  
The user may leave at any time, but if they stay longer than an hour, they must **succeed on a DC 20 Intelligence save** or begin **forgetting their own existence**, piece by piece.

### *The Beckoning Shadow*
*Wondrous Item, Legendary (Cursed)*  
A shadow that **does not belong** to its owner. It moves **slightly out of sync**, flickers unnaturally, and sometimes appears to **look back** at them.  
Once per day, the user may **step into their shadow**, vanishing into complete darkness for up to 1 minute. While inside, they are **untouchable**—but each use gives the shadow **more autonomy**.  
If used more than three times, the shadow **does not return** when they step out, continuing to move on its own.

### *The Maw Beneath the Floorboards*
*Wondrous Item, Artifact*  
A **gap** in the world that should not be. It can be placed **on any flat surface**, and when activated, the surface **opens** into a black void filled with **teeth and whispers**.  
Once per day, the user may **feed something** to the Maw. In return, they may ask it **a single question**, which it will answer in **a voice they almost recognize**.  
However, each time it is fed, **the Maw grows larger**.

### *The Last Door*
*Wondrous Item, Artifact*  
A **black wooden door**, freestanding in an empty frame. It does not open.  
Each time the user **asks the door a question**, they hear a voice whisper from the other side. The door knows **everything**, but it **never tells the truth directly**—it twists words, gives riddles, and offers **half-truths** that always lead to unintended consequences.  
One day, the door **will open on its own**. The user will not be able to stop it.

## Vestigium Magic Items – Eldritch Anomalies III

### *The Book That Reads You*
*Wondrous Item, Rare*  
A leather-bound tome with **no title and no known author**. When opened, its pages begin filling with text, describing **the reader’s thoughts, memories, and fears** in real-time.  
If the book is read for more than 10 minutes, it begins to **reveal secrets even the reader did not know**, exposing events that may not have happened—yet.

### *The Hunger Stone*
*Wondrous Item, Very Rare (Cursed)*  
A smooth, black stone that feels **warm to the touch**. When held, it **saps the user’s hunger and thirst**, allowing them to survive without food or drink.  
However, once attuned, the user must **feed the stone instead**—giving it **one memory per week**. Memories sacrificed this way are **permanently erased**, leaving only a vague sense of loss.

### *The Doorframe to Nowhere*
*Wondrous Item, Legendary*  
A lone **wooden frame** that stands without a wall. When walked through, the user arrives in **a different version of their world**—a place where one thing has **changed irreversibly**.  
The user may return at will, but each time they do, **the doorframe shifts slightly**, leading somewhere stranger with every use.

### *The Coin That Shouldn’t Exist*
*Wondrous Item, Rare*  
A **rusted coin** with no markings. When flipped, it **never lands**—it simply vanishes, reappearing **somewhere nearby within 24 hours**.  
Each time it is used, something minor **in the world changes**, unnoticed by all but the user.

### *The Tapestry of Forgotten Names*
*Wondrous Item, Very Rare*  
A massive, unraveling tapestry **stitched with thousands of names**. When a name is spoken aloud while touching the fabric, the person who bears that name **forgets who they are** for 24 hours.  
If the name is spoken **three times**, the person is **forgotten by the world entirely**, as if they never existed.

### *The Silent Violin*
*Wondrous Item, Rare*  
A stringless violin carved from **pale bone**. When drawn across the air, it plays **a sound only the dead can hear**.  
Once per long rest, the user may **play the violin for 1 minute**, drawing the attention of **all spirits within one mile**. Some come to listen.  
Others come to **remember what it was like to be alive.**

### *The Bone of a Forgotten God*
*Wondrous Item, Legendary*  
A **massive, hollow bone**, too large to be from any known creature. When held, it hums faintly with **a heartbeat that is not your own**.  
Placing an ear to the bone allows the user to **hear whispers from an ancient being**—a deity long erased from history. The more the user listens, the **louder** the whispers become.

### *The Candle That Burns Backward*
*Wondrous Item, Rare*  
A melted candle that **never drips wax**. When lit, time **reverses** in a small area for as long as the flame remains burning.  
If the candle burns for more than 10 minutes, it begins to **undo reality itself**, causing people to **forget why they exist**.

### *The Watch Without Hands*
*Wondrous Item, Very Rare*  
A gold pocket watch with **no hands on its face**. When stared at for too long, time becomes **fluid**—seconds stretch into hours, and days pass in moments.  
Once per long rest, the user may **skip ahead in time**, instantly moving to the next meaningful event. However, **memories of the skipped time are permanently lost**.

### *The Mouth in the Wall*
*Wondrous Item, Legendary (Cursed)*  
A crack in any surface that, when listened to closely, **whispers secrets in an unknown language**.  
If fed an object, it **removes all evidence that the object ever existed**. If fed a name, the person associated with it **loses all memories of their own identity**.  
If fed a living creature… **the whispering stops for one full minute before resuming, louder than before.**

### *The Tear That Never Falls*
*Wondrous Item, Rare*  
A **single drop of water**, suspended in midair, **unable to fall**. When touched, it grants the user **a vision of something that has never happened**, yet feels undeniably real.  
Each time the vision is invoked, the tear **grows slightly larger**. When it finally falls, **something will arrive with it.**

### *The Ancestral Echo*
*Wondrous Item, Very Rare*  
A small, smooth stone that **echoes with countless voices** when held. Once per long rest, the user may **call upon an ancestor**, asking them one question.  
However, the voice that answers is **not always the one that was called.**  

### *The Ash That Remembers Fire*
*Wondrous Item, Uncommon*  
A small handful of **cold, black ash** that, when scattered, **replays the last moments of what burned** to create it.  
The visions are **vivid and unrelenting**, showing not just fire, but the **pain, fear, and regret** of whatever was lost.

### *The Name That Should Not Be Spoken*
*Wondrous Item, Artifact (Cursed)*  
A scrap of parchment containing **a single word**, written in ink that writhes as if alive.  
If read aloud, **everything changes**—memories shift, history rearranges itself, and **the reader's past is rewritten** to have always known the word.  
None who have spoken it **remember who they used to be.**

## Vestigium Magic Items – Eldritch & Anomalous Erotica

### *The Lingering Caress*
*Wondrous Item, Rare*  
A silk glove that **remembers touch**. When used to touch a person, the sensation lingers for hours, growing **warmer and more intimate** with time.  
Once per long rest, the user may invoke **a past touch**, causing the subject to **relive the emotions they felt at that moment**—pleasure, longing, fear, or even betrayal.

### *The Mirror That Watches*
*Wondrous Item, Very Rare*  
A handheld mirror that **never reflects the present**. Instead, it shows **past moments of intimacy**, even those forgotten.  
If two people gaze into it together, they see **what they most desire from each other**, whether they admit it or not.  
Once per day, the mirror may show **a future that might be**, hinting at a fate entwined with longing and consequence.

### *The Kiss That Never Ends*
*Wondrous Item, Rare*  
A carved stone mouth, cold to the touch, yet oddly lifelike. When pressed to a person’s lips, they feel **an invisible kiss** follow them for the next 24 hours—gentle, urgent, or possessive depending on their own desires.  
Each time the subject **rejects or ignores** the phantom sensation, they must succeed on a **DC 15 Wisdom saving throw** or find themselves **yearning for a touch that isn’t real**.

### *The Thread of Entanglement*
*Wondrous Item, Very Rare*  
A thin, red thread, warm like **living skin**. When tied between two people, it **binds their sensations together**—what one feels, the other does as well.  
This link is permanent until either party **cuts the thread**, though doing so causes **one final surge of shared sensation**, amplified beyond mortal comprehension.

### *The Murmuring Silk*
*Wondrous Item, Rare (Cursed)*  
A sheer, shimmering veil that clings to the body like a second skin. When worn, it **whispers softly**, murmuring praise, desires, and secrets in an unknowable language.  
Once per day, the user may command the veil to **change shape**, becoming any outfit—or nothing at all. However, each use **draws more whispers**, and one day, the voice will **whisper back**.

### *The Unfinished Embrace*
*Wondrous Item, Very Rare (Cursed)*  
A phantom presence lingers in this tattered robe, wrapping around the wearer in moments of solitude. It offers **comfort, warmth, and longing**, but never speaks.  
Once attuned, the wearer **cannot bear to remove it**—any attempt to do so causes **a deep and unexplainable sadness**, as if something precious is being lost forever.

### *The Echo of a Moan*
*Wondrous Item, Rare*  
A black pearl that **remembers pleasure**. When held tightly, it emits a **faint sound**, repeating the last breath, sigh, or cry of pleasure spoken near it.  
If placed against a person’s skin, it fills them with **the remnants of another’s bliss**, causing their body to react as if reliving the sensation.

### *The Candle of Endless Yearning*
*Wondrous Item, Very Rare*
