A creature that fails a **Wisdom saving throw** is **assigned a new life.**
- They forget **who they were** and assume a new **corporate-approved persona.**
- They believe they have always held this **false identity.**
- Any attempt to **convince them otherwise fails** unless *Wish* or *Greater Restoration* is used.

**Class:** Cleric, Wizard

### **Dissonant Gestation**
*4th-level Necromancy (Ritual)*

**Casting Time:** :: 1 hour
**Range:**        :: Touch
**Components:**   :: V, S, M (a handful of grave dirt, pressed into the skin)
**Duration:**     :: Permanent (until birth or surgical removal)

You **implore the dark corners of reality** to place **an unseen burden within a creature’s body**—not a pregnancy, but an **unnatural gestation**, a thing that **grows, waits, and feeds.**

- The target must make a **Constitution saving throw**. On a failure, something **begins to gestate inside them**, though it **is not a living creature** as they understand it.
- **Each week, roll a d6** to determine the **nature of the thing growing within:**
- **1 | Bone Nesting** – The target’s bones begin **splitting, reforming, and growing redundantly**, fusing in painful, alien configurations.
- **2 | Chitinous Hatchery** – Their **flesh hardens into a shell**, and something **moves beneath it**. It will hatch, but no one knows what.
- **3 | Hollow Incubation** – The target’s organs begin to **disappear, one by one**, yet they remain alive, feeling the empty space within.
\page
- **4 | Blood Evolution** – Their blood is **no longer theirs**, but something **else’s**, moving independently, making them a host for an unseen parasite.
- **5 | Neural Infestation** – The target begins hearing **a second set of thoughts** inside their mind. These are **not theirs.** They whisper secrets.
- **6 | Aberrant Bloom** – Strange **tendrils or appendages** occasionally emerge from the target’s body, retreating before they can be seen.

**Ending the Spell:**
- If left untreated, **at the end of three months, the thing inside them will be born.** The result **is not predictable, and it may not be survivable.**
- The only way to remove the gestation **is through surgery or another, more powerful anomaly.**

**Anomaly Effect:**
- If multiple creatures are affected by this spell **in the same location**, their gestating entities **begin to sync**, forming a single, **distributed intelligence between all hosts**.

**Class:** Cleric, Warlock, Wizard

*3rd-level transmutation*

**Casting Time:** :: 1 action
**Range:**        :: 30 feet (up to 3 creatures)
**Components:**   :: V, S, M (a vial of cloned stem cells)
**Duration:**     :: Concentration, up to 1 minute

Up to three creatures in range **regain 1d8 HP at the start of each of their turns**. If they are missing any limbs, this spell initiates slow regrowth over **1d4 days.**

### **Divine Kink Role**
*2nd-level Enchantment (Ritual)*

**Casting Time:** :: 1 action
**Range:**        :: 10 feet
**Components:**   :: V, S, M (a single drop of wax, melted upon skin)
**Duration:**     :: Instantaneous

A slow, commanding whisper slithers into the target’s mind, **coaxing hidden truths** from the folds of their subconscious. This spell does not merely extract information—it **offers a temptation, a push toward self-recognition**.

- The target **experiences a moment of revelation**, as if **tied, bound, or in a position of control**, feeling their **innate alignment** within dominance-submission dynamics.
- Instead of a simple **saving throw**, the target chooses how to **react**:
- **Resist** (Wisdom saving throw) – The vision **fades**, leaving an unsettling, unfinished feeling (+1 to Insight checks against future enchantment spells).
- **Acknowledge the sensation** – The target **remembers this moment vividly**, with no immediate effect but lingering thoughts.
- **Embrace it fully** – For the next 24 hours, **other creatures using persuasion or seduction against them have advantage**, as their subconscious remains **more attuned to external control.**

This spell does not impose anything—**it merely offers the door, and the target chooses whether to walk through**.

**Class:** Bard, Warlock, Wizard

### **Existence Audit**
*9th-level divination*

**Casting Time:** :: 1 minute
**Range:**        :: 60 feet
**Components:**   :: V, S, M (a ledger containing the target’s history)
**Duration:**     :: Permanent

A deep metaphysical **review of reality** determines if the target **should continue existing.**

The target must make a **Charisma saving throw** against your spell save DC. On a failure, **they are erased from history**, their presence **retroactively removed** from records, memories, and physical existence.

- If the target has a **Legendary Resistance**, they must expend all uses before being allowed to make a saving throw.
- Creatures with a **Divine Spark, Anchored Soul, or Absolute Presence** automatically succeed.
- If the target is erased, **any lingering effects they caused remain, but their origin becomes unknown or rewritten.**

**Reality Contingency (Fail-Safe Check):**
- If a powerful entity (CR 20+) is erased, the DM may invoke a **Contested Reality Check**, where the fabric of existence resists the erasure.
- On a failure, the spell still works, but **paradox anomalies may occur**, creating unintended consequences.

**Scaling (Weaker Targets):**
- When cast at **7th level**, the target must be **CR 15 or lower** to be erased.
- When cast at **8th level**, the target must be **CR 20 or lower.**
- At **9th level**, the spell works on any target that fails the save.

**Class:** Cleric, Wizard

### **Existence Audit**
*9th-level divination*

**Casting Time:** :: 1 minute
**Range:**        :: 60 feet
**Components:**   :: V, S, M (a ledger containing the target’s history)
**Duration:**     :: Permanent

The target must make a **Charisma saving throw**. On a failure, they are **retroactively erased from history**—no records, memories, or traces of their existence remain. Their equipment, personal effects, and any impacts they made on reality remain, but **they are gone from time itself.**

**Paranormal Consequences:**
- The caster **suffers paranormal instability** for **1d10 days**, during which they experience *glitches in reality* (random sensory hallucinations, time distortions, or whispers from the void).
- Casting this spell **draws the attention of an entity known as “The Auditor.”** Within 1d6 weeks, a paranormal force **investigates** whether the spell was justified. If not, it may attempt to restore the erased target—or worse, erase the caster in return.

**Class:** Cleric, Wizard

### **Famine Birth**
*3rd-level Necromancy (Ritual)*

**Casting Time:** :: 1 action
**Range:**        :: Touch
**Components:**   :: V, S, M (a shard of cracked bone, buried in the target’s flesh)
**Duration:**     :: Until the anomaly resolves itself

You press your fingers against the target’s abdomen and **whisper an incantation that only hunger understands**. The body responds, but not in the way it should. Something **takes root within the target’s form**, but it is not life—it is absence made flesh.

- The target must make a **Constitution saving throw**. On a failure:
- **They become host to an Unborn Hunger**, a parasitic void that **feeds upon them instead of growing.**
- Each long rest, they lose **1d4 maximum hit points**, their flesh pulling taut over their bones.
- Their appetite vanishes—no matter what they eat, their body **refuses to digest it**.
- **They can feel it moving inside them**, shifting with breath, curling beneath the ribs.
- If reduced to 0 HP while afflicted, **they do not die**. Instead, their body becomes **an empty husk**, and something **else** uses their form.

**Ending the Spell:**
- If the host wishes to remove it, they must **cut it out manually**, taking **4d6 slashing damage** and making a **DC 15 Constitution check** to remain conscious.
- **A failed removal attempt** may cause the entity to **take full control, wearing the host like a suit of skin.**

**Anomaly Effect:**
- If multiple creatures are afflicted at once, they **begin to crave each other**, drawn together by an instinct to **consume the unborn within one another.**

**Class:** Cleric, Warlock, Wizard

### **Fascination**
*Cantrip Enchantment*

**Casting Time:** :: 1 action
**Range:**        :: 12 feet
**Components:**   :: V, S, M (a biometric signature of the target)
**Duration:**     :: Concentration, up to 1 minute

A subdermal neurological impulse is implanted in the target’s **cognitive prioritization center**, making them **incapable of focusing on anything but the caster**.

The target must make a **Wisdom saving throw**. On a failed save:
\page
- The affected target **follows the caster wherever they go**, unable to take their eyes off them.
- If attacked, the target enters a **berserk fury**, attacking anyone **who obstructs their pursuit** of the caster (+1 to hit, -1 AC).
- The target may **repeat the saving throw at the end of each of its turns**, ending the effect on a success.

**Class:** Bard, Warlock, Wizard

- **Materials heated in the void fire behave unpredictably:**
- Metal **becomes malleable at touch**, allowing smiths to work **without heavy tools**—but it resists shaping if it "does not like" the intended form.
- Wood **does not burn**, but **warps as though alive**, resisting nails and glue.
- Bone **fuses with metal**, creating chimeric materials that may carry unknown properties.
- The heat **does not dissipate**—crafted items remain warm for **days after forging**, pulsing with unnatural warmth.

**Anomaly Effect:**
- If overused, the **forge itself begins to change**, its anvil and tools growing **veins of unknown black metal**, refusing to create mundane items.

### **Immutable Clause**
*3rd-level Transmutation*

**Range:**        :: Touch
\page
**Components:**   :: V, S, M (a quill dipped in paradox ink)
**Duration:**     :: Permanent (until nullified)

With a whispered invocation, you **impose absolute certainty** upon an event, ensuring it **cannot be undone, altered, or reversed** by normal means.

- When cast, you declare **one simple factual state** affecting an object, person, or event. This fact **becomes legally binding in the fabric of reality**.
- Examples include:
- "This door was never locked."
- "She was always employed here."
- "This bullet did not hit me."
- The effect **cannot be dispelled, countered, or challenged** by **ordinary magic**.
- A **court-level anomaly nullification hearing** (or a **5th-level dispel magic** cast in a place of corporate power) is required to break the clause.

**Anomaly Effect:**
- If abused, the spell might **accidentally add extra clauses**, creating unintended loopholes.

### **Mandatory Compliance Policy**
*2nd-level Enchantment*

**Casting Time:** :: 1 action
**Range:**        :: 30 feet
**Components:**   :: V, S, M (a printed contract, signed in ink)
**Duration:**     :: Concentration, up to 10 minutes

You invoke a **mandatory compliance policy**, compelling a creature to **act in accordance with an official directive**.

- The target must make a **Charisma saving throw**. On a failure, they must follow a **simple command** (e.g., "deliver this package," "leave the premises," "cease operations").
- Unlike traditional enchantments, the **target rationalizes their compliance** within a **corporate, legal, or procedural framework**.
- If the command **violates established company policy** (or contradicts the target’s contract obligations), they **automatically succeed** on the saving throw.
- The spell **fails entirely** if there is no plausible procedural justification for the action.

**Anomaly Effect:**
- If overused, an **invisible compliance officer** (an unknown corporate entity) may begin tracking the caster’s **"compliance history,"** leading to **unexpected legal ramifications**.

**Class:** Bard, Warlock, Wizard

### **Manifest Anomalous Cataclysm**
*9th-level transmutation*

**Casting Time:** :: 1 action
**Range:**        :: 300 feet (1-mile-radius event)
**Components:**   :: V, S, M (a classified A.S.T.R.A.L. document)
**Duration:**     :: 24 hours

You **awaken a dormant anomaly**, unleashing an **event-scale paranormal disaster**.

- **Reality in the area distorts**, causing gravity fluctuations, spatial rifts, and shifting architecture.
- **Anomalous creatures and hazards begin manifesting**, acting unpredictably.
- **Any spell cast within the zone has a 50% chance of unexpected effects.**

**Scaling (Upcast Effect):**
- If cast at **10th level**, the **effect becomes permanent**, transforming the area into a **quarantined anomaly site.**

**Class:** Wizard, Sorcerer

The weapon deals force or slashing damage (your choice) equal to 1d8 + your spellcasting modifier.

### **Maw of the Forgotten**
*3rd-level Transmutation*

**Casting Time:** :: 1 action
**Range:**        :: Self
**Components:**   :: V, S, M (a swallowed tooth, not your own)
**Duration:**     :: Concentration, up to 1 minute

A **grinning slit** opens across your stomach, chest, or throat—an **extra mouth that was never meant to be there.** The **Maw of the Forgotten** does not hunger for food, but for **concepts, names, and existence itself.**

- As a **bonus action**, you may attempt to **devour an aspect of reality** from a creature you can see within **10 feet**. The target must make a **Charisma saving throw**. On a failure:
- They **forget their own name** for 24 hours.
- Any titles, contracts, or legal records referring to them **become unreadable**, as though they were never written.
- They suffer **disadvantage on all identity-based interactions**, including deception and persuasion.
- **Each time the Maw feeds, it grows larger, whispering secrets only you can hear.**

**Ending the Spell:**
- If the caster **does not feed it at least once per minute**, the **Maw becomes hungry**, forcing the caster to **make an Intelligence saving throw or forget their own past.**
- Once the spell ends, the mouth does not fully disappear—it remains as **scar tissue, aching whenever something forgotten lingers nearby.**

**Anomaly Effect:**
- **If cast on the same target twice, they may cease to exist entirely**, their body remaining but their **presence erased.**

**Class:** Warlock, Wizard

A shimmering, **paper-thin bureaucratic field** surrounds you, causing any attack rolls against you to suffer **disadvantage** unless the attacker:
- Spends a turn **"filing paperwork"** (taking no actions).
- **Waits in line** (losing 10 feet of movement).

**Class:** Cleric, Wizard, Artificer

### **Red Tape Binding**
\page
*2nd-level evocation*

**Casting Time:** :: 1 action
**Range:**        :: 15 feet
**Components:**   :: V, S, M (a signed document)
**Duration:**     :: Concentration, up to 1 minute

A tangle of **paperwork, bureaucratic seals, and spectral ink ribbons** ensnare the target. The creature must make a **Dexterity saving throw** or take **3d6 force damage** and be **restrained** for the duration. A restrained target can use an action to make a **Strength (Athletics) check** against your spell save DC to break free.

**At Higher Levels.** When cast using a spell slot of 3rd level or higher, the damage increases by **1d6 per level.**

**Class:** Wizard, Warlock, Cleric

### **Redacted Identity**
*4th-level abjuration*

**Casting Time:** :: 1 action
**Range:**        :: Touch
**Components:**   :: V, S, M (a bureaucratic form with the target’s name scribbled out)
**Duration:**     :: 8 hours

The target becomes **invisible to corporate tracking systems**, bureaucratic enchantments, and any **name-based surveillance or contracts**. While under this effect:

- **Their name cannot be spoken, written, or recorded by magical or technological means.**
- Any ongoing **corporate conditioning, memory alteration, or legal bindings** affecting them are **suppressed** for the duration.
- Spells such as **Compliance Protocol, Digital Summons, or Memory Fragmentation** **fail outright** if cast on the target.
- Entities attempting to recall or reference the target experience **glitching cognitive dissonance**, causing them to hesitate or forget minor details about them.

If the target **signs a contract or willingly identifies themselves**, the spell **immediately ends**.

**Class:** Wizard, Cleric, Warlock

You distort a single spoken word, causing it to be completely omitted from a sentence. This does not change meaning but leaves an obvious gap, as if the speaker momentarily forgot the word or it was intentionally censored. If used against a spellcaster, their spell is unaffected, but they experience a brief moment of dissonance.

**Range:**        :: Touch
**Components:**   :: V, S, M (a biometric ID chip)
**Duration:**     :: Permanent (until revoked)

A **state-issued biological override** ensures **total reproductive regulation**, granting or preventing fertility based on **anomalous genetic programming or corporate mandates**.

- You must **register the procedure** within a recognized **biological oversight agency** or an equivalent **A.S.T.R.A.L. fertility governance database**.
- The recipient’s **reproductive ability is altered per official documentation**—either **activated, suspended, or set on a predetermined cycle**.
- A recipient may **petition for reversal**, requiring an **administrative appeal and 48-hour processing delay.**
\page
- Attempts to **circumvent the procedure** (via dispel magic or natural means) trigger **an automatic health verification scan**, possibly flagging the recipient for investigation.

**Anomaly Effect:**
- In rare cases, **biological data corruption** results in **spontaneous genetic mutations**—some with **unpredictable side effects**.

**Class:** Cleric, Wizard

### **Residual Imprint**
*2nd-level Necromancy*

**Casting Time:** :: 1 action
**Range:**        :: 30 feet

You touch a surface and **pull residual emotions, whispered words, and sensory echoes** from its past. These are not spirits, but **impressions left by heightened emotions**—love, fear, guilt, rage.

- As long as you concentrate, you experience **faded flashes** of what transpired in the location over the last **24 hours** (or up to **10 years for a higher-level cast**).
- You may **see blurred faces, hear indistinct voices, or feel the emotions of the past occupants**.
- If a **violent crime** was committed here, the spell may **temporarily create an echo**, repeating the event **as a flickering hallucination** that others can witness.

- If overused in one place, the imprints **might notice you back**, becoming **aware that they are being observed**.

### **Skin Unwoven**
*4th-level Necromancy*

**Casting Time:** :: 1 action
**Range:**        :: 30 feet
**Components:**   :: V, S, M (a thread soaked in human blood)
**Duration:**     :: Concentration, up to 1 minute

You weave **an invisible suture in the air**, connecting it to the target’s **flesh and nerves**. The thread does not cut, it **unravels**, pulling the skin away in delicate layers.

- The target must make a **Constitution saving throw**. On a failure, their **flesh begins to separate from their body, piece by piece.**
- **Round 1:** Their fingertips and lips **begin to curl and peel**, exposing raw flesh.
- **Round 2:** The **skin along their arms and jaw pulls loose**, hanging like discarded parchment.
- **Round 3:** Their entire **face and chest are stripped**, leaving **only muscle and exposed nerves.**
\page
- The target takes **2d8 necrotic damage per round** and suffers **disadvantage on all Dexterity-based actions due to agony.**
- **If the spell lasts the full minute, the target is left entirely skinless**, a raw, quivering thing, forced to exist in **constant, unbearable sensation.**

**Ending the Spell:**
- If the target **succeeds the saving throw on any turn**, their skin stops peeling, but what has been lost **remains lost**.
- A target that **loses all their skin** must be **ritually stitched back together**, requiring **a surgeon and a week of recovery.**

**Anomaly Effect:**
- If cast repeatedly, the **peeled skin may attempt to reform itself into something separate,** crawling and watching from the corners of the room.

**Class:** Warlock, Wizard

### **Summon the Saint (Ritual)**
*6th-level conjuration (ritual)*

**Casting Time:** :: 1 hour
**Range:**        :: Touch
**Components:**   :: V, S, M (a black candle, a silver coin, and the target’s written name on parchment)
**Duration:**     :: Permanent until fulfilled

You invoke the **Assassins of the Saint**, a hidden order of executioners bound by ancient contracts. This spell **marks a target for death**, ensuring that **they will never know peace again**.

- **At dawn the next day, the target awakens with a blood-red rose placed on their chest.**
- From this moment, **Assassins of the Saint** will begin hunting them.
- The **first assassin arrives within 1d6 days**, with each subsequent hunter increasing in lethality.

**Counterplay & Removal:**
- The **mark cannot be dispelled** through normal means.
- Only by making an **offering of equal or greater worth** (to the Saint’s order) can the mark be **transferred** to another soul.

**The Saint’s Will is Absolute:**
If the caster **attempts to interfere**, they too receive the **mark of the blood rose**.

**Class:** Cleric, Warlock, Wizard

### **Surveillance Blackout**
*4th-level illusion*

**Casting Time:** :: 1 action
**Range:**        :: 30 feet
**Components:**   :: V, S, M (a cracked camera lens)
**Duration:**     :: 10 minutes

You create an **anomalous interference field** that disrupts **all surveillance and recording devices** within range.
- **Security cameras, sensors, and microphones malfunction**, either looping old footage, displaying static, or going completely dark.
- **Magical scrying attempts have disadvantage**, as their feed becomes distorted and unreliable.
- **Observers viewing the affected area remotely** must succeed on a **Wisdom saving throw** or be **unable to recall what they saw**.

This spell **does not grant invisibility** but renders technological and magical observation **highly unreliable.**

**Class:** Wizard, Rogue, Bard

### **Synaptic Reset**
*6th-level abjuration*

**Casting Time:** :: 1 action
**Range:**        :: Touch
**Components:**   :: V, S, M (a lightning-infused crystal)
**Duration:**     :: Instantaneous

You generate a **controlled bioelectric discharge** that **resets all neurological activity**, eliminating unwanted effects.

- **Removes all mind-affecting conditions**, including **Fear, Confusion, Domination, and Mental Overload.**
- If the target has been **altered by an anomaly or corporate augmentation**, they may make a **Constitution saving throw** to **resist its influence for 1 hour.**
- If used on an **unwilling** target, they must make a **Constitution saving throw** or become **Stunned for 1 minute.**

**Class:** Cleric, Wizard

### **System Breach**
*5th-level transmutation*

**Casting Time:** :: 1 action
**Range:**        :: Touch
**Components:**   :: V, S, M (a broken firewall key)
**Duration:**     :: Concentration, up to 1 minute

You touch a **wall, vault, or reinforced door**, rewriting its properties to allow passage.
- **Solid matter bends away from you**, creating a **10-foot tunnel** through any non-magical material.
- If the surface is reinforced or warded, make an **Arcana check (DC 20)** to bypass it.
- The tunnel remains until the spell ends.

**Class:** Artificer, Wizard

### **System Reboot**
*7th-level transmutation*

**Casting Time:** :: 1 action
**Range:**        :: Touch
\page
**Components:**   :: V, S, M (a shattered data drive)
**Duration:**     :: Instantaneous

You **reset** the target’s physical and mental state. They **remove all levels of exhaustion, regain 50 hit points, and end one curse, disease, or madness.** However, they forget the last **hour** of their memories.

**Class:** Cleric, Wizard

### **Tactical Enhancement Protocol**
*2nd-level transmutation*

**Casting Time:** :: 1 action
**Range:**        :: 30 feet
**Components:**   :: V, S, M (a data uplink or HUD visor)
**Duration:**     :: 1 minute

You optimize a creature’s response time. The target’s **speed doubles**, they gain a **+2 bonus to AC**, have **advantage on Dexterity saving throws**, and **gain an additional action** on each turn (Attack, Dash, Disengage, Hide, or Use an Object). When the spell ends, the target is **unable to move or take actions for one round** due to neural lag.

**Class:** Artificer, Wizard

You rewind a creature’s biological clock by **1d10 minutes**. This **removes wounds, conditions, or death effects** that occurred within that time. The spell does not restore missing limbs.

You create an invisible, arcane **barrier of denial** in a **20-foot cube**. Creatures attempting to teleport, phase, or cross into the area must make a **Charisma saving throw**. On a failure, they are **forcibly bounced back** to their point of origin and take **4d6 force damage**.

*3rd-level evocation*

You convert **arcane energy into an analog signal**, allowing you to transmit a spoken message or magical effect through radio waves, telegraph lines, or wired technology. Spells like *message* and *sending* can be cast **across vast distances if a signal relay exists.**

### **The Backdoor**

**Range:**        :: Self (1 mile)
**Components:**   :: V, S, M (a key that no longer fits any lock)
**Duration:**     :: Instantaneous

You **step through an unseen access point** and reappear inside **any place you have entered before**, such as a **locked building, hidden room, or secured facility**.

**Class:** Warlock, Wizard

### **The Bleeding Contract**
*5th-level Enchantment*

**Casting Time:** :: 1 hour
**Range:**        :: Touch
**Components:**   :: V, S, M (a quill, blood, and a binding sigil)
**Duration:**     :: Permanent (until terms are fulfilled)

You draft a **supernatural contract**, binding the signee to **a deal they cannot escape**—either willingly or through **legal loopholes within reality itself**.

- The target must **willingly sign the contract** (or fail a **Wisdom saving throw** if coerced).
- The contract **must specify exact terms** (e.g., "deliver this artifact," "never betray the company," "act as my informant").
- If the signee **fails to uphold the contract**, they begin **hemorrhaging lifeforce (1d6 psychic damage per hour)** until the terms are fulfilled.
- The contract is **self-enforcing**—no outside intervention can alter its terms without a **corporate tribunal or anomaly adjustment**.

**Anomaly Effect:**
- If poorly worded, the **contract may self-interpret**, leading to **unintended consequences** that the caster did not foresee.

**Class:** Warlock, Wizard

### **The Crawling Hunger**
*4th-level Enchantment*

**Casting Time:** :: 1 action
**Range:**        :: 30 feet
**Components:**   :: V, S, M (a shard of gnawed bone)
**Duration:**     :: Permanent (until satiated)

You **place a consuming need inside a creature**, but it is not hunger for food—it is for **something worse.**
\page

- The target must make a **Wisdom saving throw**. On a failure, they develop an **insatiable hunger** for **a specific, forbidden thing**, chosen randomly from the list below:
- **1 | Flesh of the Living** – The target craves human flesh. **They can resist, but only barely.**
- **2 | Dead Voices** – The target wants to **chew on books, scrolls, and paper**, consuming knowledge instead of food.
- **3 | Their Own Body** – The target begins **biting and gnawing at their own hands, arms, and lips** when no one is looking.
- **4 | Glass and Metal** – They find themselves chewing on **shards of glass and rusted nails**, feeling neither pain nor damage—but never satisfaction.
- **5 | Forgotten Names** – The target whispers **the names of those who have been erased from history**, consuming their legacies with each repetition.
- **6 | Shadows** – They try to eat **lightless spaces**, their mouth opening wider than it should when they stand in darkness.

- The **hunger cannot be resisted forever**—every **24 hours without consuming the object, they take 2d6 psychic damage.**
- If they give in, they **feel no satisfaction, only greater hunger**.

**Anomaly Effect:**
- If multiple creatures are cursed in the same location, **they begin to crave each other, driven to a shared consumption.**

**Class:** Warlock, Wizard

### **The Hollow Man’s Smile**
*3rd-level illusion*

**Casting Time:** :: 1 action
**Range:**        :: Self
**Components:**   :: V, S, M (a mask that has never been worn)
**Duration:**     :: 1 hour

You conjure an **unnerving mask** over your face, obscuring your true identity.

- You gain **advantage on Deception checks**, but all social interactions become **deeply unsettling**.
- **Creatures who see you for more than 1 minute must make a Wisdom saving throw (DC 15)** or develop a **deep fear of you** for the next 24 hours.

**Class:** Bard, Warlock, Wizard

### **The Price of Names**

**Casting Time:** :: 1 minute
**Range:**        :: 30 feet
**Components:**   :: V, S, M (a scrap of paper with the target’s name)
**Duration:**     :: 1 week

You strip power from a target’s **true name**, making them vulnerable.

- The target has **disadvantage on all saving throws against magic that references them by name**.
- Anyone who **speaks their name aloud** can sense their direction **within 1 mile**.
- This effect remains **until the name is burned, rewritten, or changed**.

**Class:** Cleric, Warlock, Wizard

### **The Specter’s Invitation**

You invite a spirit back into the world of the living, but only for a limited time.

- The summoned spirit **returns in physical form** for 24 hours.
- They **remember everything** from their death and are aware that **this is temporary**.
- At the end of the spell’s duration, the spirit **knows who summoned them—and may not be happy about it.**

**Class:** Cleric, Warlock, Wizard

- **The target gains +1 to AC and saving throws** while the spell is active.
- At any time within 24 hours, the Ticking Man may **call in the favor**, forcing the target to perform **one action or request, no matter the cost**.
- If the request is refused, **the target immediately ages 2d20 years** and loses the benefits of the spell.

This spell is **often misused in underground establishments**, enhancing **paid experiences or delivering unexpected sensations.**

### **Unscheduled Maintenance**
*2nd-level Conjuration*

**Casting Time:** :: 1 action
**Range:**        :: 30 feet
**Components:**   :: V, S, M (a neon "CLOSED" sign)
**Duration:**     :: 1 hour

A targeted **building, passageway, or technological system** becomes **temporarily shut down for "repairs"**, creating an **official-looking lockdown**.

- **Doors will not open**, cameras **cease recording**, and security systems **display a “DOWN FOR MAINTENANCE” error**.
- Employees or passersby will **subconsciously believe the closure is valid** unless they succeed on a **DC 15 Intelligence check**.

**Anomaly Effect:**
- If cast **too often**, bureaucratic forces **may send an actual maintenance crew**, unknowingly reinforcing the spell.

**Class:** Bard, Wizard, Rogue

*3rd-level Necromancy*

**Casting Time:** :: 1 action
**Range:**        :: Touch

You press your lips against the target’s **pulse**, whispering a silent invocation to something waiting in the dark.

- The target **loses 2 HP per round**.
- The caster **absorbs 1 HP per round**, if not already at full health.
- If the target reaches 0 HP this way, they **do not die immediately**—instead, they feel a presence **leaning over them, breathing against their ear, waiting**.

**Class:** Bard, Warlock, Wizard

### **Veilborn Glimmer**
*Cantrip Illusion*

**Casting Time:** :: 1 action
**Range:**        :: Self
**Components:**   :: S, V
**Duration:**     :: 1 minute

Your body shimmers with ethereal light, briefly phasing between reality and the unknown. For the duration, you can dim or brighten your own appearance at will, causing yourself to glow faintly (shedding dim light in a 5-foot radius) or become shadowed (light sources within 10 feet of you appear dimmer). This effect ends if you fall unconscious or dismiss it as a bonus action.

**Class:** Bard, Warlock, Wizard

### **Veins of the Forgotten**
*3rd-level Transmutation*

**Casting Time:** :: 1 action
**Range:**        :: Self
**Components:**   :: V, S, M (a drop of your own blood, mixed with ink)
**Duration:**     :: 1 minute

You **allow your veins to forget their purpose**, turning your circulatory system into something **liquid, shifting, and unknowable**.

- For the duration of the spell, your **blood is no longer entirely inside you**—it slithers **beneath your skin, forming moving patterns**, and drips onto the floor in places you haven't stepped.
- You gain the following benefits and consequences:
- **Your body is semi-fluid**, allowing you to **squeeze through gaps no wider than 1 inch**.
- **You are immune to poison and diseases**, as your blood is no longer organic.
- **You take half damage from slashing attacks**, but **piercing attacks deal double damage** as your body cannot hold shape properly.
- **Each time you cast a spell, your blood reacts violently**, causing you to lose **1d6 HP per spell level**.
- **If you reach 0 HP while this spell is active, you do not die**—instead, your blood **scatters across the room**, and your body must be **reassembled manually**.

**Anomaly Effect:**
- If used too frequently, your blood **refuses to return to your body**, forming **an independent entity that watches you, waiting for an opportunity to replace you.**

**Class:** Warlock, Wizard

### **Verdict of the Forgotten**
*6th-level necromancy*

**Casting Time:** :: 1 action
**Range:**        :: 60 feet
**Components:**   :: V, S, M (a relic of an erased historical figure)
**Duration:**     :: Concentration, up to 1 minute

You invoke **a judgment long forgotten**, compelling reality itself to erase the target. The target must make a **Charisma saving throw**. On a failure, they take **10d10 necrotic damage**, and all creatures within **30 feet** must make a Wisdom saving throw or be **frightened for 1 minute**.

If the target is reduced to 0 HP by this spell, their body **disintegrates into nothing**, and their existence is stricken from minor recorded history (casual memories fade, but deep records remain).

At Higher Levels. When you cast this spell using a spell slot of 7th level or higher, the damage increases by **1d10 per slot level above 6th**.

**Class:** Cleric, Wizard

All creatures in range are cured of **diseases, infections, and parasitic infestations.** If a creature is actively

suffering from a necrotic or viral-based curse, this spell grants **advantage on saving throws against it for the next 24 hours.**

**Components:**   :: V, S, M (a defibrillator or mechanical equivalent)

You restore a creature to life, provided it has been dead for no longer than 1 minute. The creature returns with 1 hit point, but its body bears an unnatural stiffness, as if something is keeping it running rather than fully reviving it. Until they complete a long rest, they gain one level of exhaustion.

### **Wardrobe Malfunction**
*Cantrip Transmutation*

**Casting Time:** :: 1 action
**Range:**        :: 10 feet
**Components:**   :: V, S
**Duration:**     :: Instantaneous

This spell **remotely adjusts clothing fastenings**, loosening, tightening, or reconfiguring **zippers, buttons, laces, or corset ties** at will.

- If cast subtly, creatures must succeed on a **Wisdom (Insight) check** against your spell save DC to notice the alteration.
- If cast on an unwilling creature, they may attempt a **Dexterity saving throw** to resist the effect.
- At **higher levels**, this spell **can affect armored fastenings**, requiring a **Strength check** (DC 15) to remove manually.

**Class:** Bard, Sorcerer, Wizard

### **Wisp of the Forgotten**
*Cantrip Necromancy*

**Casting Time:** :: 1 action
**Range:**        :: 30 feet
**Components:**   :: S, V
**Duration:**     :: 1 minute

You conjure a faint, ghostly whisper from beyond the veil, carrying an unintelligible but haunting message to a creature within range. The target must succeed on a Wisdom saving throw or become unnerved until the start of its next turn, giving it disadvantage on the next Wisdom (Perception) check or initiative roll it makes. If the creature is already frightened, it takes psychic damage equal to your spellcasting ability modifier.

**Class:** Bard, Warlock, Wizard

### **Witness of the Veil**
*5th-level divination*

**Casting Time:** :: 1 action
**Range:**        :: 60 feet
**Components:**   :: V, S, M (an unblinking glass eye)
**Duration:**     :: Concentration, up to 10 minutes

You force a target to see **what should remain unseen**.

- The target must make a **Wisdom saving throw (DC 17)** or become **paranoid**, seeing shadowy figures lurking just beyond their vision.
- While paranoid, the target has **disadvantage on Perception checks** and must roll a **d6 at the start of each turn**:
- **1–3:** The hallucinations whisper terrible secrets, causing **2d8 psychic damage**.
- **4–6:** The target acts normally but remains unnerved.

The effect ends early if the target **passes three consecutive Wisdom saves** or if a **greater restoration** is cast.

**Class:** Cleric, Warlock, Wizard

### **Womb of the Unwritten**
*2nd-level Transmutation (Ritual)*

**Casting Time:** :: 10 minutes
**Range:**        :: Touch
**Components:**   :: V, S, M (a drop of void-infused ink, absorbed into the skin)
**Duration:**     :: Permanent (until the anomaly resolves itself)

You whisper **an incantation not meant for mortal tongues**, invoking the presence of something **that waits between fate and flesh**. The spell rewrites the **biological continuity of the target’s reproductive essence**, severing it from natural law and entangling it with the unknown.

- Upon casting, the target must roll a **d6**—their fate is dictated by an unseen force:
\page
- **1-2 | Fertility Erasure** – The target is **forgotten by the lineage of time**; they can no longer conceive, and **records of their ancestry begin to fade from existence**.
- **3-4 | Unstable Genesis** – The target’s fertility is **unpredictably altered**, capable of conception or sterility depending on **external anomalies**—moon phases, forgotten dreams, or the whispers of something in the walls.
- **5 | Fractured Inheritance** – Any offspring conceived by the target will inherit **memories, scars, or traits from an unknown progenitor**, one that never lived yet has always existed.
- **6 | The Unborn Take Root** – The target experiences a **phantasmal pregnancy**, feeling the weight of something growing within them—yet no child is ever born, only a presence that lingers in their shadow.

- The change is **not immediately noticed**—it takes effect **subtly, like a whisper embedded in the fabric of their being**.
- Any attempt to **reverse the effect** without understanding it risks **creating a secondary anomaly**, potentially rewriting the target’s **entire genetic structure**.

**Anomaly Effect:**
- If the spell is interrupted mid-cast, **all present individuals are momentarily connected by a shared bloodline**, as if they were part of an unseen genealogical tree that should not exist.

**Class:** Cleric, Wizard
